### Activities: list

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/docs/activities/list

Returns a list of channel activity events that match the request criteria. For example, you can retrieve events associated with a particular channel or with the user's own channel.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/activities

### Description
Returns a list of channel activity events that match the request criteria. For example, you can retrieve events associated with a particular channel or with the user's own channel.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/activities

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - The part parameter specifies the activity resource parts that the API response will include. Valid values are id, snippet, and contentDetails.
- **channelId** (string) - Optional - The channelId parameter specifies the unique ID of the channel for which the activity list should be retrieved.
- **home** (boolean) - Optional - The home parameter specifies whether the API should return activities that are relevant to the user.
- **maxResults** (integer) - Optional - The maxResults parameter specifies the maximum number of results to return.
- **mine** (boolean) - Optional - The mine parameter specifies whether the API should return activities that the user has performed.
- **pageToken** (string) - Optional - The pageToken parameter identifies a specific page of results to return.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "example": "GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/activities?part=snippet&channelId=UC_x5XG1OV2P6uZZ5FSM9Ttw"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **kind** (string) - The type of resource.
- **etag** (string) - The ETag of the response.
- **nextPageToken** (string) - The token that can be used to retrieve the next page of results.
- **pageInfo** (object) - Paging details for the returned list of results.
  - **totalResults** (integer) - The total number of results available on all pages.
  - **resultsPerPage** (integer) - The number of results included in this response.
- **items** (array) - A list of activities that match the request criteria.
  - **kind** (string) - The type of resource.
  - **etag** (string) - The ETag of the response.
  - **id** (string) - The ID of the activity.
  - **snippet** (object) - The snippet object contains basic details about the activity.
    - **publishedAt** (string) - The time at which the activity was published.
    - **channelId** (string) - The ID of the channel where the activity occurred.
    - **title** (string) - The title of the activity.
    - **description** (string) - The description of the activity.
    - **thumbnails** (object) - The thumbnails associated with the activity.
    - **channelTitle** (string) - The title of the channel where the activity occurred.
    - **type** (string) - The type of the activity.
    - **detailCount** (integer) - The number of details associated with the activity.
  - **contentDetails** (object) - The contentDetails object contains details about the content of the activity.
    - **upload** (object) - Contains details about an uploaded video activity.
      - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the uploaded video.
    - **like** (object) - Contains details about a like activity.
      - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the video that was liked.
    - **favorite** (object) - Contains details about a favorite activity.
      - **resourceId** (object) - The resource ID object contains details about the resource that was favorited.
        - **kind** (string) - The type of the resource.
        - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the video that was favorited.
    - **comment** (object) - Contains details about a comment activity.
      - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the video that was commented on.
      - **commentId** (string) - The ID of the comment.
    - **playlistItem** (object) - Contains details about a playlist item activity.
      - **playlistId** (string) - The ID of the playlist.
      - **playlistItemId** (string) - The ID of the playlist item.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "example": {
    "kind": "youtube#activityList",
    "etag": "string",
    "pageInfo": {
      "totalResults": 100,
      "resultsPerPage": 5
    },
    "items": [
      {
        "kind": "youtube#activity",
        "etag": "string",
        "id": "string",
        "snippet": {
          "publishedAt": "2023-01-01T12:00:00Z",
          "channelId": "UC_x5XG1OV2P6uZZ5FSM9Ttw",
          "title": "New video uploaded",
          "description": "Check out my latest video!",
          "thumbnails": {},
          "channelTitle": "Google Developers",
          "type": "upload",
          "detailCount": 1
        },
        "contentDetails": {
          "upload": {
            "videoId": "dQw4w9WgXcQ"
          }
        }
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

### Errors
- **400 Bad Request**: Invalid request.
- **401 Unauthorized**: Invalid authentication credentials.
- **403 Forbidden**: The request is understood, but it has been refused.
- **404 Not Found**: The requested resource could not be found.
- **500 Internal Server Error**: Internal server error.
```

--------------------------------

### Retrieve Video Resource and Filter Fields (YouTube Data API v3)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/getting-started

This example demonstrates how to retrieve a video resource and further refine the response using the 'fields' parameter. It includes 'snippet' and 'statistics' parts but uses 'fields=items(id,snippet,statistics)' to exclude 'kind' and 'etag' properties from the response.

```URL
https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/videos?id=7lCDEYXw3mM&key=YOUR_API_KEY&part=snippet,statistics&fields=items(id,snippet,statistics)
```

### GET /channels - List the authenticated user's channel

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/code_samples/code_snippets

Retrieves the channel data for the authorized user's YouTube channel.

```APIDOC
## GET /channels

### Description
Retrieves the channel data for the authorized user's YouTube channel.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/channels

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **mine** (boolean) - Required - Indicates that the API should only return channels owned by the user authorizing the request.
- **part** (string) - Optional - Specifies the channel resource parts that the API response should include.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "example": "GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/channels?part=snippet&mine=true"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **items** (array) - Contains channel resource objects.
  - **snippet** (object) - Contains basic information about the channel.
    - **title** (string) - The title of the channel.
    - **description** (string) - The channel's description.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "example": {
    "kind": "youtube#channelListResponse",
    "etag": "...",
    "items": [
      {
        "kind": "youtube#channel",
        "etag": "...",
        "id": "YOUR_CHANNEL_ID",
        "snippet": {
          "title": "Your Channel Name",
          "description": "Your channel description."
        }
      }
    ]
  }
}
```
```

### GET /activities

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/docs/activities

Retrieves a list of channel activity events that match the request criteria. This can be used to get events associated with a particular channel or the user's own channel.

```APIDOC
## GET /activities

### Description
Returns a list of channel activity events that match the request criteria. For example, you can retrieve events associated with a particular channel or with the user's own channel.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/activities

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **alt** (string) - Optional - Specifies the data format for the response. Supported values are json.
- **fields** (string) - Optional - YouTube Data API uses partial responses, which allows you to retrieve only the fields you need.
- **key** (string) - Optional - Your API key.
- **maxResults** (unsigned integer) - Optional - The maximum number of results to return.
- **mine** (boolean) - Optional - Set this to true to return activities for the currently authenticated user.
- **pageToken** (string) - Optional - The page token associated with the page of results to retrieve.
- **part** (string) - Required - The part of the activity resource that you want the activity resource to include in the response. The valid parts are `snippet` and `contentDetails`.
- **channelId** (string) - Optional - Returns the activities associated with the specified channel. This parameter is used with the `mine` parameter. If the `mine` parameter is set to true, then the `channelId` parameter will specify the channel that the authenticated user is acting as.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "example": "GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/activities?part=snippet%2CcontentDetails&mine=true&key=YOUR_API_KEY"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **kind** (string) - Specifies the type of the resource. This value always set to youtube#activity.
- **etag** (string) - The ETag of the response.
- **id** (string) - The ID of the activity.
- **snippet** (object) - The snippet object contains basic details about the activity, including the channel ID, title, description, published time, and thumbnails.
  - **publishedAt** (datetime) - The time at which the activity was published.
  - **channelId** (string) - The ID of the channel associated with the activity.
  - **title** (string) - The title of the activity.
  - **description** (string) - The description of the activity.
  - **thumbnails** (object) - A set of thumbnails associated with the activity.
  - **channelTitle** (string) - The title of the channel associated with the activity.
  - **type** (string) - The type of the activity (e.g., 'upload', 'favorite', 'like', 'comment', 'subscription', 'social').
  - **groupId** (string) - The ID of the group that the activity belongs to.
- **contentDetails** (object) - The contentDetails object contains details about the content of the activity, such as the video ID, playlist ID, or social post information.
  - **upload** (object) - Details about an uploaded video activity.
    - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the uploaded video.
  - **like** (object) - Details about a liked resource activity.
    - **resourceId** (object) - The resourceId object contains details about the resource that was liked.
      - **kind** (string) - The type of the resource (e.g., 'youtube#video').
      - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the video that was liked.
  - **favorite** (object) - Details about a favorited resource activity.
    - **resourceId** (object) - The resourceId object contains details about the resource that was favorited.
      - **kind** (string) - The type of the resource (e.g., 'youtube#video').
      - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the video that was favorited.
  - **comment** (object) - Details about a comment activity.
    - **resourceId** (object) - The resourceId object contains details about the resource associated with the comment.
      - **kind** (string) - The type of the resource (e.g., 'youtube#video').
      - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the video the comment was made on.
      - **channelId** (string) - The ID of the channel the comment was made on.
  - **subscription** (object) - Details about a subscription activity.
    - **resourceId** (object) - The resourceId object contains details about the channel that was subscribed to.
      - **kind** (string) - The type of the resource (e.g., 'youtube#channel').
      - **channelId** (string) - The ID of the channel that was subscribed to.
  - **playlistItem** (object) - Details about a playlist item activity.
    - **resourceId** (object) - The resourceId object contains details about the playlist item.
      - **kind** (string) - The type of the resource (e.g., 'youtube#video').
      - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the video that was added to the playlist.
    - **playlistId** (string) - The ID of the playlist.
    - **playlistItemId** (string) - The ID of the playlist item.
  - **recommendation** (object) - Details about a recommendation activity.
    - **resourceId** (object) - The resourceId object contains details about the recommended resource.
      - **kind** (string) - The type of the resource (e.g., 'youtube#video').
      - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the recommended video.
      - **channelId** (string) - The ID of the channel associated with the recommendation.
    - **reason** (string) - The reason for the recommendation.
    - **seedResourceId** (object) - The resourceId object for the seed resource that led to the recommendation.
      - **kind** (string) - The type of the resource (e.g., 'youtube#video').
      - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the recommended video.
      - **channelId** (string) - The ID of the channel associated with the recommendation.
      - **playlistId** (string) - The ID of the playlist associated with the recommendation.
  - **social** (object) - Details about a social post activity.
    - **type** (string) - The type of social post (e.g., 'tweet').
    - **resourceId** (object) - The resourceId object contains details about the social post.
      - **kind** (string) - The type of the resource (e.g., 'youtube#video').
      - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the video associated with the social post.
      - **channelId** (string) - The ID of the channel associated with the social post.
      - **playlistId** (string) - The ID of the playlist associated with the social post.
    - **author** (string) - The author of the social post.
    - **referenceUrl** (string) - The URL of the social post.
    - **imageUrl** (string) - The URL of the image associated with the social post.
  - **channelItem** (object) - Details about a channel item activity.
    - **resourceId** (object) - The resourceId object contains details about the channel item.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "example": {
    "kind": "youtube#activityList",
    "etag": "etag",
    "items": [
      {
        "kind": "youtube#activity",
        "etag": "etag",
        "id": "activity-id",
        "snippet": {
          "publishedAt": "2023-10-27T10:00:00Z",
          "channelId": "channel-id",
          "title": "Video Uploaded",
          "description": "A new video has been uploaded.",
          "thumbnails": {
            "default": {
              "url": "https://example.com/default.jpg",
              "width": 120,
              "height": 90
            }
          },
          "channelTitle": "Channel Name",
          "type": "upload",
          "groupId": "group-id"
        },
        "contentDetails": {
          "upload": {
            "videoId": "video-id"
          }
        }
      }
    ]
  }
}
```
```

### Upload Video using C# and YouTube API v3

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/code_samples/dotnet

This snippet demonstrates uploading a video to YouTube using C#. It requires the Google API Client Library for .NET and a `client_secrets.json` file for authentication. The code handles video metadata, privacy settings, and provides progress updates during the upload.

```csharp
using System;
using System.IO;
using System.Reflection;
using System.Threading;
using System.Threading.Tasks;

using Google.Apis.Auth.OAuth2;
using Google.Apis.Services;
using Google.Apis.Upload;
using Google.Apis.Util.Store;
using Google.Apis.YouTube.v3;
using Google.Apis.YouTube.v3.Data;

namespace Google.Apis.YouTube.Samples
{
  /// <summary>
  /// YouTube Data API v3 sample: upload a video.
  /// Relies on the Google APIs Client Library for .NET, v1.7.0 or higher.
  /// See https://developers.google.com/api-client-library/dotnet/get_started
  /// </summary>
  internal class UploadVideo
  {
    [STAThread]
    static void Main(string[] args)
    {
      Console.WriteLine("YouTube Data API: Upload Video");
      Console.WriteLine("==============================");

      try
      {
        new UploadVideo().Run().Wait();
      }
      catch (AggregateException ex)
      {
        foreach (var e in ex.InnerExceptions)
        {
          Console.WriteLine("Error: " + e.Message);
        }
      }

      Console.WriteLine("Press any key to continue...");
      Console.ReadKey();
    }

    private async Task Run()
    {
      UserCredential credential;
      using (var stream = new FileStream("client_secrets.json", FileMode.Open, FileAccess.Read))
      {
        credential = await GoogleWebAuthorizationBroker.AuthorizeAsync(
            GoogleClientSecrets.Load(stream).Secrets,
            // This OAuth 2.0 access scope allows an application to upload files to the
            // authenticated user's YouTube channel, but doesn't allow other types of access.
            new[] { YouTubeService.Scope.YoutubeUpload },
            "user",
            CancellationToken.None
        );
      }

      var youtubeService = new YouTubeService(new BaseClientService.Initializer()
      {
        HttpClientInitializer = credential,
        ApplicationName = Assembly.GetExecutingAssembly().GetName().Name
      });

      var video = new Video();
      video.Snippet = new VideoSnippet();
      video.Snippet.Title = "Default Video Title";
      video.Snippet.Description = "Default Video Description";
      video.Snippet.Tags = new string[] { "tag1", "tag2" };
      video.Snippet.CategoryId = "22"; // See https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/docs/videoCategories/list
      video.Status = new VideoStatus();
      video.Status.PrivacyStatus = "unlisted"; // or "private" or "public"
      var filePath = @"REPLACE_ME.mp4"; // Replace with path to actual movie file.

      using (var fileStream = new FileStream(filePath, FileMode.Open))
      {
        var videosInsertRequest = youtubeService.Videos.Insert(video, "snippet,status", fileStream, "video/*");
        videosInsertRequest.ProgressChanged += videosInsertRequest_ProgressChanged;
        videosInsertRequest.ResponseReceived += videosInsertRequest_ResponseReceived;

        await videosInsertRequest.UploadAsync();
      }
    }

    void videosInsertRequest_ProgressChanged(Google.Apis.Upload.IUploadProgress progress)
    {
      switch (progress.Status)
      {
        case UploadStatus.Uploading:
          Console.WriteLine("{0} bytes sent.", progress.BytesSent);
          break;

        case UploadStatus.Failed:
          Console.WriteLine("An error prevented the upload from completing.\n{0}", progress.Exception);
          break;
      }
    }

    void videosInsertRequest_ResponseReceived(Video video)
    {
      Console.WriteLine("Video id '{0}' was successfully uploaded.", video.Id);
    }
  }
}

```

### Quota Cost Updates and Migration Guide

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-tw

On June 18, 2014, descriptions for API methods were updated with quota costs. A new migration guide was also introduced to help users move from YouTube Data API v2 to v3.

```APIDOC
### Quota Cost Updates (June 18, 2014)
- API method descriptions now include their respective quota costs.
- Resource part definitions specify the quota cost for retrieving each part.
- Example: `subscriptions.insert` has a quota cost of ~50 units. The `subscription` resource parts (`snippet`, `contentDetails`, `subscriberSnippet`) each cost 2 units.
- **Note**: Quota costs are subject to change without notice.

### Migration Guide
- A new guide, "Migrating Your Application to YouTube Data API (v3)", is available.
- It explains how to use the v3 API for functionality previously available in the v2 API.
- This guide is intended for applications still using the v2 API, which was deprecated on March 4, 2014.
```

--------------------------------

### HTTP GET Request for MembershipsLevels

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/docs/membershipsLevels/list

This code snippet demonstrates the HTTP GET request to retrieve membership levels for a YouTube channel. It requires the `part` parameter, which specifies the desired resource properties (`id` and/or `snippet`). The request must be authorized with the `youtube.channel-memberships.creator` scope.

```http
GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/membershipsLevels?part=snippet
```

### Python Example for channelBanners.insert Method

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=tr

Demonstrates how to insert channel banners using Python with the YouTube Data API v3. This snippet covers the necessary steps and parameters for the channelBanners.insert method.

```Python
from googleapiclient.discovery import build

# Assume 'youtube' is an authenticated YouTube API service object
youtube = build('youtube', 'v3', developerKey='YOUR_API_KEY') # Replace with your authenticated client

with open('path/to/your/banner.jpg', 'rb') as f:
    media_body = f.read()

request = youtube.channelBanners().insert(
    channelId='UCxxxxxxxxxxxxxx', # Replace with your channel ID
    body={},
    media_body=media_body
)

try:
    response = request.execute()
    print("Channel banner uploaded successfully:", response)
except Exception as e:
    print(f"An error occurred: {e}")

```

--------------------------------

### Get Channel Information by Handle

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=tr

The `channels.list` method now supports a new `forHandle` parameter, allowing you to retrieve channel information by specifying the YouTube handle.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/channels (channels.list)

### Description
Retrieves a collection of channels that match the specified query parameters, including by YouTube handle.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/channels

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - The `part` parameter specifies the channel resource parts that the API response will include. Valid values are: `contentDetails`, `brandingSettings`, `topicDetails`, `snippet`, `statistics`, `status`, `invideoPromotion`, `auditDetails`, `contentOwnerDetails`.
- **forHandle** (string) - Required - A YouTube handle, starting with '@', for which to retrieve the channel information.

### Request Example
```
GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/channels?part=snippet&forHandle=@YouTubeDevs
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **items** (array) - A list of channel resources that match the request. Each item contains the requested `part` details.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "kind": "youtube#channelListResponse",
  "etag": "ETAG",
  "pageInfo": {
    "totalResults": 1,
    "resultsPerPage": 1
  },
  "items": [
    {
      "kind": "youtube#channel",
      "etag": "ETAG",
      "id": "CHANNEL_ID",
      "snippet": {
        "title": "YouTube Developers",
        "description": "Official channel for YouTube API and developer resources.",
        "customUrl": "@YouTubeDevs",
        "publishedAt": "2007-02-14T00:00:00Z",
        "thumbnails": {
          "default": {"url": "URL"},
          "medium": {"url": "URL"},
          "high": {"url": "URL"}
        },
        "localized": {
          "title": "YouTube Developers",
          "description": "Official channel for YouTube API and developer resources."
        },
        "country": "US"
      }
    }
  ]
}
```
```

--------------------------------

### Retrieve My Uploads

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/code_samples/go

This endpoint retrieves a list of videos uploaded to the channel associated with the authenticated request. It uses `playlistItems.list` and `channels.list` to get the uploaded videos.

```APIDOC
## Retrieve My Uploads

### Description
This endpoint retrieves a list of videos uploaded to the channel associated with the authenticated request. It uses `playlistItems.list` and `channels.list` to get the uploaded videos.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/playlistItems (used in conjunction with channels.list to get upload playlist ID)

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - Specifies the parts of the playlist item resource to retrieve (e.g., "snippet").
- **playlistId** (string) - Required - The ID of the playlist that contains the uploaded videos.
- **mine** (boolean) - Required (for channels.list) - Set to `true` to retrieve the channel associated with the authenticated user.

### Request Example
```go
// Example using Go client library
// Assumes 'service' is an authenticated *youtube.Service object

// First, get the upload playlist ID for the authenticated user's channel
channelsResponse := service.Channels.List("contentDetails").Mine(true).Do()
playlistId := channelsResponse.Items[0].ContentDetails.RelatedPlaylists.Uploads

// Then, retrieve playlist items from the upload playlist
playlistItemsResponse := service.PlaylistItems.List("snippet").PlaylistId(playlistId).Do()

for _, item := range playlistItemsResponse.Items {
    fmt.Printf("%s (%s)\n", item.Snippet.Title, item.Snippet.ResourceId.VideoId)
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **items** (array) - A list of playlist item resources.
  - **snippet** (object) - The snippet object containing details like title, video ID, etc.
    - **title** (string) - The title of the video.
    - **resourceId** (object)
      - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the video.

#### Response Example
```json
{
 "kind": "youtube#playlistItemListResponse",
 "etag": "...",
 "nextPageToken": "...",
 "items": [
  {
   "kind": "youtube#playlistItem",
   "etag": "...",
   "id": "...",
   "snippet": {
    "publishedAt": "...",
    "channelId": "...",
    "title": "My Awesome Video",
    "description": "...",
    "thumbnails": { ... },
    "channelTitle": "...",
    "playlistId": "...",
    "position": 0,
    "resourceId": {
     "kind": "youtube#video",
     "videoId": "dQw4w9WgXcQ"
    }
   }
  }
 ]
}
```
```

- `channels.update`
- `videos.getRating`

### YouTube Data API v3 - Partial Resources

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/getting-started

Explains how to use the `part` and `fields` parameters to retrieve only the necessary resource properties, improving efficiency.

```APIDOC
## YouTube Data API v3 - Partial Resources

### Description
The API supports retrieving partial resources to minimize data transfer, parsing, and storage. This is achieved using the `part` and `fields` parameters.

### Parameters
- **`part`**: Identifies groups of properties to be returned for a resource.
- **`fields`**: Filters the API response to return only specific properties within the requested resource parts.
```

--------------------------------

### GET /youtube/v3/channels

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=vi

Retrieves information about channels, including branding settings.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/channels

### Description
Retrieves information about one or more YouTube channels. This endpoint can also return the `brandingSettings` part, which includes text and images for a channel's page.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/channels

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - Specifies the `channel` resource parts that the API response will include. Comma-separated list. Can include `brandingSettings`.
- **id** (string) - Optional - The ID of the channel to retrieve.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "part": "snippet,brandingSettings",
  "id": "CHANNEL_ID"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200 OK)
- **items** (array) - A list of channel resources.
  - **brandingSettings** (object) - Settings for the channel's branding.
    - **channel** (object) - Channel-specific branding settings.
      - **keywords** (string) - Channel keywords.
      - **description** (string) - Channel description.
      - **ownerCountry** (string) - The country of the channel owner.
    - **image** (object) - Image-related branding settings.
      - **bannerExternalUrl** (string) - URL of the channel banner.
      - **faviconUrl** (string) - URL of the channel favicon.

#### Error Response
- **errors** (array) - Description of the error encountered.
```

### List Uploaded Videos

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/docs/playlistItems/list

This endpoint allows you to retrieve a list of videos uploaded to the authenticated user's channel. It first fetches the channel details to get the uploads playlist ID, and then lists the items within that playlist.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/channels

### Description
Retrieves channel details, including the playlist ID for uploaded videos.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/channels

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **mine** (boolean) - Required - Set to `true` to retrieve the channel of the authenticated user.
- **part** (string) - Required - Specifies the parts of the channel resource to retrieve. Use `contentDetails` to get playlist information.

### Request Example
```
GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/channels?mine=true&part=contentDetails
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **items** (array) - Contains channel resource details.
  - **contentDetails** (object) - Contains details about the channel's content.
    - **relatedPlaylists** (object) - Contains playlist IDs for various channel content types.
      - **uploads** (string) - The playlist ID for videos uploaded to the channel.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "items": [
    {
      "contentDetails": {
        "relatedPlaylists": {
          "uploads": "UUxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx"
        }
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

## GET /youtube/v3/playlistItems

### Description
Retrieves a list of items in a specified playlist. Used here to list uploaded videos.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/playlistItems

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **playlistId** (string) - Required - The ID of the playlist to retrieve items from (e.g., the uploads playlist ID).
- **part** (string) - Required - Specifies the parts of the playlist item resource to retrieve. Use `snippet` to get video title and ID.
- **maxResults** (integer) - Optional - The maximum number of results to return.
- **pageToken** (string) - Optional - The token for the next page of results.

### Request Example
```
GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/playlistItems?playlistId=UUxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx&part=snippet&maxResults=50
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **items** (array) - Contains playlist item resources.
  - **snippet** (object) - Contains the snippet of the playlist item.
    - **title** (string) - The title of the video.
    - **resourceId** (object) - Contains the resource ID of the playlist item.
      - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the video.
- **nextPageToken** (string) - The token to retrieve the next page of results, or null if there are no more pages.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "items": [
    {
      "snippet": {
        "title": "My Awesome Video",
        "resourceId": {
          "videoId": "dQw4w9WgXcQ"
        }
      }
    }
  ],
  "nextPageToken": "CAUQAA"
}
```
```

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=tr

Searches for resources in YouTube, such as videos, channels, and playlists.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/search

### Description
Searches for YouTube resources.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/search

### Parameters

- **channelId** (string) - Optional - Restricts the search to the specified channel.
- **q** (string) - Required - The search query.
- **type** (string) - Optional - The type of resources to search for (e.g., "video", "channel", "playlist").

  "q": "Google",
  "channelId": "UC_x5XG1OV2P6uZZ5FSM9Ttw",

      "id": {
        "kind": "youtube#video",
        "videoId": "..."
      },
      "snippet": {
        "title": "Google I/O 2021"
      }
    }
  ]
}

### GET /channels

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=th

```APIDOC
## GET /channels

### Description
Retrieves channel data. You can retrieve this data by including `invideoPromotion` in the `part` parameter value.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/channels

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - Comma-separated list of channel resource parts to retrieve. Include `invideoPromotion` to get in-video promotion data.
- **id** (string) - Required - The ID of the channel to retrieve.

### Request Example
```
GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/channels?part=invideoPromotion&id=CHANNEL_ID
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **items** (array) - An array of channel resources.
  - **id** (string) - The ID of the channel.
  - **invideoPromotion** (object) - The in-video promotion data for the channel.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "kind": "youtube#channelListResponse",
  "etag": "ETAG_VALUE",
  "items": [
    {
      "kind": "youtube#channel",
      "etag": "ETAG_VALUE",
      "id": "CHANNEL_ID",
      "invideoPromotion": {
        "items": [
          {
            "id": "PROMOTION_ID",
            "content": {
              "type": "video",
              "videoId": "VIDEO_ID"
            },
            "position": {
              "type": "overlay",
              "offsetMs": 1000,
              "durationMs": 5000,
              "cornerLayer": "topRight"
            }
          }
        ]
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

### GET /youtube/v3/videos - videos.update Update

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=th

Clarifications regarding the `snippet.publishedAt` and `status.publishAt` properties for the `videos.update` method, including how they are populated and requirements when setting `status.publishAt`.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/videos - videos.update

### Description
Applies changes to the video identified by the video ID.

### Method
POST (or PUT)

### Endpoint
`/youtube/v3/videos`

### Request Body Parameters
- **snippet.publishedAt** (string) - The date and time that the video was published. This value may be different than the time that the video was uploaded. For example, if a video is uploaded as a private video and then made public at a later time, the property value specifies the time that the video was made public. The updated definition also explains how the value is populated for private and unlisted videos.
- **status.publishAt** (string) - If you set this property's value when calling the `videos.update` method, you must also set the `status.privacyStatus` property value to `private` even if the video is already private.
```

### Retrieve Video Resource Excluding Specific Parts (YouTube Data API v3)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/getting-started

This example shows how to retrieve a video resource while excluding certain parts from the response. By setting the 'part' parameter to 'snippet,statistics', the 'contentDetails' and 'status' parts are omitted. Default properties like 'kind' and 'etag' are still included.

```URL
https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/videos?id=7lCDEYXw3mM&key=YOUR_API_KEY&part=snippet,statistics
```

## GET /youtube/v3/channels

### Description

GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/channels

- **part** (string) - Required - Specifies a comma-separated list of properties to return.

    - **title** (string) - The title of the channel.
    - **description** (string) - The channel's description.
  - **statistics** (object) - Contains statistics about the channel.
    - **subscriberCount** (integer) - The number of subscribers to the channel (rounded down to three significant figures if > 1000).

  "kind": "youtube#channelListResponse",
  "etag": "_ABCDEFG1234567890",
  "items": [

      "kind": "youtube#channel",

      },
      "statistics": {

### Set Thumbnail - Java

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-tw

Provides a Java example for setting a video thumbnail using the thumbnails.set method. This requires the video ID and the path to the thumbnail image file.

```Java
import com.google.api.client.googleapis.json.GoogleJsonResponseException;
import com.google.api.client.http.javanet.NetHttpTransport;
import com.google.api.client.json.jackson2.JacksonFactory;
import com.google.api.services.youtube.YouTube;
import com.google.api.services.youtube.model.ThumbnailSetResponse;

import java.io.IOException;
import java.io.File;

public class SetThumbnail {

    private static YouTube youtube;

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        // This is a placeholder. You need to set up your YouTube service.
        // Example initialization (requires authentication):
        // youtube = new YouTube.Builder(new NetHttpTransport(), new JacksonFactory(), credential)
        //         .setApplicationName("youtube-set-thumbnail-example")
        //         .build();

        System.out.println("Placeholder for Java code example for thumbnails.set");

        // Example usage:
        // String videoId = "YOUR_VIDEO_ID";
        // File thumbnailFile = new File("path/to/your/thumbnail.jpg");
        // try {
        //     setThumbnail(videoId, thumbnailFile);
        // } catch (IOException e) {
        //     e.printStackTrace();
        // }
    }

    private static void setThumbnail(String videoId, File thumbnailFile) throws IOException {
        if (youtube == null) {
            System.err.println("YouTube service not initialized.");
            return;
        }

        try {
            System.out.println("Setting thumbnail for video: " + videoId);
            YouTube.Thumbnails.Set request = youtube.thumbnails().set(videoId, "high", thumbnailFile);
            ThumbnailSetResponse response = request.execute();
            System.out.println("Thumbnail set successfully.");
            // The response might contain details about the available thumbnails.
        } catch (GoogleJsonResponseException e) {
            System.err.println("GoogleJsonResponseException : " + e.getDetails());
            e.printStackTrace();
        } catch (IOException e) {
            System.err.println("IOException: " + e.getMessage());
            e.printStackTrace();
        }
    }
}

```

--------------------------------

### POST /thumbnails/set (onBehalfOfContentOwner parameter)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=vi

The `thumbnails.set` method now supports the `onBehalfOfContentOwner` parameter.

```APIDOC
## POST /thumbnails/set with onBehalfOfContentOwner

### Description
This endpoint allows you to set a custom thumbnail for a video. It now supports the `onBehalfOfContentOwner` parameter, which is relevant for users operating on behalf of a content owner.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
`/thumbnails/set`

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
None

#### Query Parameters
* **onBehalfOfContentOwner** (string) - Optional. The ID of the content owner for whom the request is being made.
* **videoId** (string) - Required. The ID of the video for which the thumbnail is being set.

#### Request Body
* **data** (string) - Required. The image data for the thumbnail. The image must be a PNG, JPG, or GIF file, with a size of 16:9 and at least 1280x720 pixels.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "videoId": "dQw4w9WgXcQ",
  "onBehalfOfContentOwner": "YOUR_CONTENT_OWNER_ID",
  "data": "base64EncodedImageData"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
* **id** (string) - The ID of the video.
* **default** (object) - Default thumbnail details.
  * **url** (string) - URL of the default thumbnail.
  * **width** (integer) - Width of the default thumbnail.
  * **height** (integer) - Height of the default thumbnail.
* **medium** (object) - Medium thumbnail details.
  * **url** (string) - URL of the medium thumbnail.
  * **width** (integer) - Width of the medium thumbnail.
  * **height** (integer) - Height of the medium thumbnail.
* **high** (object) - High-resolution thumbnail details.
  * **url** (string) - URL of the high-resolution thumbnail.
  * **width** (integer) - Width of the high-resolution thumbnail.
  * **height** (integer) - Height of the high-resolution thumbnail.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "id": "dQw4w9WgXcQ",
  "default": {
    "url": "https://i.ytimg.com/vi/dQw4w9WgXcQ/default.jpg",
    "width": 120,
    "height": 90
  },
  "medium": {
    "url": "https://i.ytimg.com/vi/dQw4w9WgXcQ/mqdefault.jpg",
    "width": 320,
    "height": 180
  },
  "high": {
    "url": "https://i.ytimg.com/vi/dQw4w9WgXcQ/hqdefault.jpg",
    "width": 480,
    "height": 360
  }
}
```
```

### Retrieve User Uploads

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/code_samples/go

Retrieves a list of videos uploaded by the authenticated user. The process involves getting the user's channel ID, identifying their uploads playlist, and iterating through the videos.

```APIDOC
## Retrieve User Uploads

### Description
This endpoint fetches all videos uploaded by the currently authenticated user. It first determines the user's channel ID, then finds the associated "uploads" playlist, and finally lists the videos within that playlist.

### Method

### Endpoint

### Response

  - **snippet** (object) - The snippet of the video.

### Update to Shorts View Counting

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=th

Starting March 31, 2025, YouTube's view counting for Shorts will change. Views will be counted when a Short starts to play or replay, without a minimum watch time requirement. This impacts the `channels.statistics.viewCount` and `videos.statistics.viewCount` fields.

```APIDOC
## Update to Shorts View Counting

### Description
Starting March 31, 2025, the way views are counted for YouTube Shorts will change. Previously, a view was counted after a certain watch duration. The new system counts a view each time a Short begins to play or is replayed, regardless of watch time. This change will be reflected in the `viewCount` statistics for both channels and videos.

### Affected Fields
- `channels.statistics.viewCount`
- `videos.statistics.viewCount`

### Effective Date
March 31, 2025
```

--------------------------------

### Retrieve YouTube Channel Uploads (C#)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/code_samples/dotnet

This snippet retrieves a list of videos uploaded to the authenticated user's YouTube channel. It requires the Google APIs Client Library for .NET and a `client_secrets.json` file for authentication. The code calls `channels.list` to get the uploads playlist ID and then `playlistItems.list` to fetch video details.

```csharp
using System;
using System.IO;
using System.Reflection;
using System.Threading;
using System.Threading.Tasks;

using Google.Apis.Auth.OAuth2;
using Google.Apis.Services;
using Google.Apis.Upload;
using Google.Apis.Util.Store;
using Google.Apis.YouTube.v3;
using Google.Apis.YouTube.v3.Data;

namespace Google.Apis.YouTube.Samples
{
  /// <summary>
  /// YouTube Data API v3 sample: retrieve my uploads.
  /// Relies on the Google APIs Client Library for .NET, v1.7.0 or higher.
  /// See https://developers.google.com/api-client-library/dotnet/get_started
  /// </summary>
  internal class MyUploads
  {
    [STAThread]
    static void Main(string[] args)
    {
      Console.WriteLine("YouTube Data API: My Uploads");
      Console.WriteLine("============================");

      try
      {
        new MyUploads().Run().Wait();
      }
      catch (AggregateException ex)
      {
        foreach (var e in ex.InnerExceptions)
        {
          Console.WriteLine("Error: " + e.Message);
        }
      }

      Console.WriteLine("Press any key to continue...");
      Console.ReadKey();
    }

    private async Task Run()
    {
      UserCredential credential;
      using (var stream = new FileStream("client_secrets.json", FileMode.Open, FileAccess.Read))
      {
        credential = await GoogleWebAuthorizationBroker.AuthorizeAsync(
            GoogleClientSecrets.Load(stream).Secrets,
            // This OAuth 2.0 access scope allows for read-only access to the authenticated 
            // user's account, but not other types of account access.
            new[] { YouTubeService.Scope.YoutubeReadonly },
            "user",
            CancellationToken.None,
            new FileDataStore(this.GetType().ToString())
        );
      }

      var youtubeService = new YouTubeService(new BaseClientService.Initializer()
      {
        HttpClientInitializer = credential,
        ApplicationName = this.GetType().ToString()
      });

      var channelsListRequest = youtubeService.Channels.List("contentDetails");
      channelsListRequest.Mine = true;

      // Retrieve the contentDetails part of the channel resource for the authenticated user's channel.
      var channelsListResponse = await channelsListRequest.ExecuteAsync();

      foreach (var channel in channelsListResponse.Items)
      {
        // From the API response, extract the playlist ID that identifies the list
        // of videos uploaded to the authenticated user's channel.
        var uploadsListId = channel.ContentDetails.RelatedPlaylists.Uploads;

        Console.WriteLine("Videos in list {0}", uploadsListId);

        var nextPageToken = "";
        while (nextPageToken != null)
        {
          var playlistItemsListRequest = youtubeService.PlaylistItems.List("snippet");
          playlistItemsListRequest.PlaylistId = uploadsListId;
          playlistItemsListRequest.MaxResults = 50;
          playlistItemsListRequest.PageToken = nextPageToken;

          // Retrieve the list of videos uploaded to the authenticated user's channel.
          var playlistItemsListResponse = await playlistItemsListRequest.ExecuteAsync();

          foreach (var playlistItem in playlistItemsListResponse.Items)
          {
            // Print information about each video.
            Console.WriteLine("{0} ({1})", playlistItem.Snippet.Title, playlistItem.Snippet.ResourceId.VideoId);
          }

          nextPageToken = playlistItemsListResponse.NextPageToken;
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
```

### Retrieve User Uploads in Go

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/code_samples/go

This Go program retrieves a list of videos uploaded by the authenticated user. It first gets the user's channel ID, then identifies their uploads playlist, and finally iterates through the videos in that playlist, displaying their titles and IDs. Requires OAuth 2.0 authorization.

```go
package main

import (
	"context"
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"net/http"

	"google.golang.org/api/option"
	"google.golang.org/api/youtube/v3"
)

func listMyUploads(client *http.Client) {
	ctx := context.Background()
	youtubeService, err := youtube.NewService(ctx, option.WithHTTPClient(client))
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Error creating YouTube client: %v", err)
	}

	// Get the authenticated user's channel ID
	userCall := youtubeService.Channels.List([]string{"contentDetails"})
	userCall.Mine(true)
	userResponse, err := userCall.Do()
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Error fetching channel details: %v", err)
	}

	if len(userResponse.Items) == 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Could not find the authenticated user's channel.")
	}

	uploadsPlaylistId := userResponse.Items[0].ContentDetails.RelatedPlaylists.Uploads

	// List videos in the uploads playlist
	playlistCall := youtubeService.PlaylistItems.List([]string{"snippet"})
	playlistCall.PlaylistId(uploadsPlaylistId)
	playlistCall.MaxResults(50) // Adjust as needed

	playlistResponse, err := playlistCall.Do()
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Error listing playlist items: %v", err)
	}

	fmt.Println("Your uploaded videos:")
	for _, item := range playlistResponse.Items {
		fmt.Printf("- Title: %s, Video ID: %s\n", item.Snippet.Title, item.Snippet.ResourceId.VideoId)
	}
}

func main() {
	// Assume getClient() from the authorization example is available and returns an authenticated *http.Client
	// ctx := context.Background()
	// client, err := getClient(ctx)
	// if err != nil {
	// 	log.Fatalf("Unable to get authenticated client: %v", err)
	// }
	// listMyUploads(client)
	fmt.Println("This is a placeholder. Call listMyUploads with an authenticated client.")
}

```

### Update on Shorts View Count (Effective March 31, 2025)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=vi

Starting March 31, 2025, YouTube's view counting method for Shorts will change. Views will be counted when a Short starts to play or replay, regardless of watch time. This change affects the `channels.statistics.viewCount` and `videos.statistics.viewCount` fields.

```APIDOC
## YouTube Shorts View Count Update

### Description
Effective March 31, 2025, the API will count views for YouTube Shorts differently. Views will be registered upon the start or replay of a Short, without a minimum watch time requirement. This update impacts the `viewCount` property within `channels.statistics` and `videos.statistics` resources.

### Method
N/A (This is a change in data reporting, not an API method)

### Endpoint
N/A

### Parameters
N/A

### Request Example
N/A

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- `channels.statistics.viewCount` (integer) - Updated view count for channels, reflecting the new Shorts view counting method.
- `videos.statistics.viewCount` (integer) - Updated view count for videos, reflecting the new Shorts view counting method.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "kind": "youtube#channelListResponse",

      "statistics": {
        "viewCount": "123456789"
      }

### YouTube API: Update Channel Settings (Python)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=vi

Shows how to update channel settings using the YouTube Data API v3 in Python. This example focuses on updating the invideo promotion settings.

```Python
from googleapiclient.discovery import build

def update_channel_invideo_promotion(youtube, channel_id, promoted_by_content_owner):
    """Updates the invideo promotion setting for a channel.

    Args:
        youtube: Authorized YouTube API service instance.
        channel_id: The ID of the channel to update.
        promoted_by_content_owner: Boolean indicating if promotion is by content owner.
    """
    try:
        # Fetch current channel settings to modify
        channel_request = youtube.channels().list(part='brandingSettings', id=channel_id)
        channel_response = channel_request.execute()

        if not channel_response.get('items'):
            print(f"Channel with ID {channel_id} not found.")
            return

        channel_snippet = channel_response['items'][0]
        branding_settings = channel_snippet.get('brandingSettings', {})
        invideo_promotion = branding_settings.get('invideoPromotion', {{}})

        invideo_promotion['promotedByContentOwner'] = promoted_by_content_owner
        branding_settings['invideoPromotion'] = invideo_promotion

        update_request = youtube.channels().update(
            part='brandingSettings',
            body={'id': channel_id, 'brandingSettings': branding_settings}
        )
        update_response = update_request.execute()
        print(f"Channel invideo promotion updated for {channel_id}.")
        return update_response

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"An error occurred: {e}")

if __name__ == '__main__':
    # Placeholder for authenticated YouTube API service
    # youtube = build('youtube', 'v3', credentials=credentials)
    # update_channel_invideo_promotion(youtube, 'YOUR_CHANNEL_ID', True)
    print("Example execution requires authenticated youtube service.")

```

### POST /thumbnails/set - onBehalfOfContentOwner Parameter

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=tr

The `thumbnails.set` method now supports the `onBehalfOfContentOwner` parameter.

```APIDOC
## POST /thumbnails/set

### Description
Uploads a thumbnail to be associated with a video. Supports the `onBehalfOfContentOwner` parameter for content owners.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
`/upload/youtube/v3/thumbnails/set`

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
N/A

#### Query Parameters
- **videoId** (string) - Required - The ID of the video with which the thumbnail should be associated.
- **onBehalfOfContentOwner** (string) - Optional - The ID of the content owner. This parameter is used only in requests made by or on behalf of a content owner.

#### Request Body
(Request body is for the media upload itself, typically multipart/form-data)

### Request Example
```
POST /upload/youtube/v3/thumbnails/set?videoId=VIDEO_ID&onBehalfOfContentOwner=CONTENT_OWNER_ID HTTP/1.1
Host: www.googleapis.com
Content-Type: multipart/form-data; boundary=BOUNDARY

--BOUNDARY
Content-Disposition: form-data; name="thumbnail"; filename="thumbnail.jpg"
Content-Type: image/jpeg

[Image data]
--BOUNDARY--
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **default** (object) - The default thumbnail. 
  - **url** (string) - The URL of the thumbnail.
- **high** (object) - The high-resolution thumbnail.
  - **url** (string) - The URL of the thumbnail.
- **medium** (object) - The medium-resolution thumbnail.
  - **url** (string) - The URL of the thumbnail.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "kind": "youtube#thumbnail",
  "etag": "...",
  "default": {
    "url": "https://i.ytimg.com/vi/VIDEO_ID/default.jpg"
  },
  "medium": {
    "url": "https://i.ytimg.com/vi/VIDEO_ID/mqdefault.jpg"
  },
  "high": {
    "url": "https://i.ytimg.com/vi/VIDEO_ID/hqdefault.jpg"
  }
}
```

### Retrieve Video Resource with Nested Field Filtering (YouTube Data API v3)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/getting-started

This example shows how to retrieve a video resource and apply granular filtering using the 'fields' parameter, including filtering nested properties within the 'snippet' object. It specifies 'snippet' and 'statistics' parts but uses 'fields=items(id,snippet(channelId,title,categoryId),statistics)' to select specific fields within the snippet.

```URL
https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/videos?id=7lCDEYXw3mM&key=YOUR_API_KEY&fields=items(id,snippet(channelId,title,categoryId),statistics)&part=snippet,statistics
```

### PUT /playlistItems

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/docs/playlistItems

Modifies a playlist item. For example, you could update the item's position in the playlist.

```APIDOC
## PUT /playlistItems

### Description
Modifies a playlist item. For example, you could update the item's position in the playlist.

### Method
PUT

### Endpoint
`/playlistItems`

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - The part of the playlist item resource that you want the API to return. Valid values are:
  - `snippet`
- **onBehalfOfContentOwner** (string) - Optional - Note: This parameter is intended for use by YouTube partners that own content and delegate management of that content to other representatives. As the onBehalfOfContentOwner parameter indicates that the request is being made on behalf of a content owner, the authenticated user must have the appropriate permissions to list content associated with that content owner. 

#### Request Body
- **id** (string) - Required - The ID of the playlist item to update.
- **snippet** (object) - Optional - The snippet object contains basic details about the playlist item.
  - **playlistId** (string) - The ID of the playlist that the item belongs to.
  - **resourceId** (object) - The ID of the resource that is included in the playlist.
    - **kind** (string) - The kind of resource.
    - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the video.
  - **position** (unsigned integer) - The position of the item in the playlist.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "example": "PUT https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/playlistItems?part=snippet&key=YOUR_API_KEY\n{\n  \"id\": \"PLAYLIST_ITEM_ID_TO_UPDATE\",\n  \"snippet\": {\n    \"position\": 2\n  }\n}"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **kind** (string) - Identifies this as a playlist item.
- **etag** (string) - The ETag of the response.
- **snippet** (object) - The snippet of the playlist item.
  - **publishedAt** (datetime) - The date and time that the item was published.
  - **channelId** (string) - The ID of the channel that the item belongs to.
  - **title** (string) - The title of the playlist item.
  - **description** (string) - The description of the playlist item.
  - **thumbnails** (object) - The thumbnails for the playlist item.
  - **channelTitle** (string) - The title of the channel that the item belongs to.
  - **videoOwnerChannelTitle** (string) - The title of the channel that owns the video.
  - **videoOwnerChannelId** (string) - The ID of the channel that owns the video.
  - **playlistId** (string) - The ID of the playlist that the item belongs to.
  - **position** (unsigned integer) - The position of the item in the playlist.
  - **resourceId** (object) - The ID of the resource that is included in the playlist.
    - **kind** (string) - The kind of resource.
    - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the video.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "example": "{\n  \"kind\": \"youtube#playlistItem\",\n  \"etag\": \"_XhBJc6jnWe2EUEj6R10_4yX_4s\",\n  \"snippet\": {\n    \"publishedAt\": \"2023-01-01T00:00:00Z\",\n    \"channelId\": \"UC-lHJZR3Gqxm24_Vd_AJsww\",\n    \"title\": \"Updated Video Title\",\n    \"description\": \"Description for the updated video.\",\n    \"thumbnails\": {\n      \"default\": {\n        \"url\": \"https://i.ytimg.com/vi/VIDEO_ID_TO_UPDATE/default.jpg\",\n        \"width\": 120,\n        \"height\": 90\n      }\n    },\n    \"channelTitle\": \"Channel Title\",\n    \"videoOwnerChannelTitle\": \"Channel Title\",\n    \"videoOwnerChannelId\": \"UC-lHJZR3Gqxm24_Vd_AJsww\",\n    \"playlistId\": \"PL_z_8Ca23ueMjI0Y2Y4YjQ3YjA\",\n    \"position\": 2,\n    \"resourceId\": {\n      \"kind\": \"youtube#video\",\n      \"videoId\": \"VIDEO_ID_TO_UPDATE\"\n    }\n  }\n}"
}
```
```

### GET /youtube/v3/members

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/docs/members/list

Retrieves a list of members for the authenticated YouTube channel. This endpoint allows filtering and pagination of member data.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/members

### Description
Retrieves a list of members for the authenticated YouTube channel. This endpoint allows filtering and pagination of member data.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/members

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - Specifies the parts of the member resource to include in the response. Typically `snippet`.
- **alt** (string) - Optional - Specifies the data format for the response. Common values are `json`.
- **fields** (string) - Optional - Specifies a subset of fields to return in the response.
- **key** (string) - Optional - Your API key.
- **maxResults** (integer) - Optional - The maximum number of results to return per page.
- **pageToken** (string) - Optional - The page token to retrieve the next page of results.
- **mode** (string) - Optional - Specifies the type of members to return. Possible values are `all_current` or `updates`.
- **hasAccessToLevel** (string) - Optional - Filters members by their access to a specific membership level ID.
- **filterByMemberChannelId** (string) - Optional - Filters members by their channel ID. Can specify multiple channel IDs separated by commas, up to a limit of 100.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "example": "GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/members?part=snippet&maxResults=5&mode=all_current&key=YOUR_API_KEY"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **kind** (string) - Identifies the API resource's type. Value will be `youtube#memberListResponse`.
- **etag** (string) - The Etag of this resource.
- **nextPageToken** (string) - The token for the next page of results.
- **pageInfo** (object) - Encapsulates paging information.
  - **totalResults** (integer) - The total number of results.
  - **resultsPerPage** (integer) - The number of results per page.
- **items** (list) - A list of members matching the request criteria.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "example": {
    "kind": "youtube#memberListResponse",
    "etag": "someEtagValue",
    "nextPageToken": "someNextPageToken",
    "pageInfo": {
      "totalResults": 100,
      "resultsPerPage": 5
    },
    "items": [
      {
        "kind": "youtube#member",
        "etag": "memberEtagValue",
        "id": "memberId1",
        "snippet": {
          "memberSince": "2023-01-01T10:00:00Z",
          "displayName": "Member One",
          "memberLevelId": "levelId1"
        }
      }
      // ... more members
    ]
  }
}
```

### Errors
- **badRequest (400)** - `channelMembershipsNotEnabled`: The creator channel does not have channel memberships enabled.
- **badRequest (400)** - `invalidMode`: The `mode` parameter value is invalid.
- **badRequest (400)** - `invalidPageToken`: The `pageToken` parameter value is invalid.
- **badRequest (400)** - `invalidHasAccessToLevel`: The `hasAccessToLevel` parameter value is invalid.
- **badRequest (400)** - `invalidFilterByMemberChannelId`: The `filterByMemberChannelId` parameter value is invalid or exceeds the limit.
```

--------------------------------

### Upload a Video to YouTube in Go

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/code_samples/go

This Go program demonstrates how to upload a video file to YouTube using the API. It requires the path to the video file and potentially other metadata. This functionality requires specific OAuth 2.0 scopes for uploading.

```go
package main

import (
	"context"
	"flag"
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"net/http"

	"golang.org/x/oauth2"
	"google.golang.org/api/option"
	"google.golang.org/api/youtube/v3"
)

func uploadVideo(client *http.Client, filePath string) {
	ctx := context.Background()
	youtubeService, err := youtube.NewService(ctx, option.WithHTTPClient(client))
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Error creating YouTube client: %v", err)
	}

	video := &youtube.Video{
		Snippet: &youtube.VideoSnippet{
			Title:       "My Awesome Video",
			Description: "This is a description of my awesome video.",
			Tags:        []string{"go", "youtube", "api", "upload"},
			CategoryId:  "22", // Example category ID for 'People & Blogs'
		},
		Status: &youtube.VideoStatus{
			PrivacyStatus: "private", // or "public", "unlisted"
		},
	}

	call := youtubeService.Videos.Insert([]string{"snippet,status"}, video)

	file, err := os.Open(filePath)
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Error opening video file: %v", err)
	}
	defer file.Close()

	response, err := call.Media(file).Do()
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Error uploading video: %v", err)
	}

	fmt.Printf("Successfully uploaded video: %s\n", response.Id)
}

func main() {
	var videoPath string
	flag.StringVar(&videoPath, "file", "", "Path to the video file to upload.")
	flag.Parse()

	if videoPath == "" {
		log.Fatal("You must provide the path to the video file using the -file flag.")
	}

	// Assume getClient() from the authorization example is available and returns an authenticated *http.Client
	// with appropriate upload scopes.
	// ctx := context.Background()
	// client, err := getClient(ctx)
	// if err != nil {
	// 	log.Fatalf("Unable to get authenticated client: %v", err)
	// }
	// uploadVideo(client, videoPath)
	fmt.Println("This is a placeholder. Call uploadVideo with an authenticated client and -file flag.")
}

```

### Retrieve User's Uploaded Videos (Ruby)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/docs/playlistItems/list

This Ruby code snippet demonstrates how to authenticate with the YouTube API and retrieve a list of videos uploaded to the authenticated user's channel. It uses the `channels.list` method to get the uploads playlist ID and then the `playlist_items.list` method to fetch and display video titles and IDs, handling pagination.

```ruby
#!/usr/bin/ruby

require 'rubygems'
gem 'google-api-client', '>0.7'
require 'google/api_client'
require 'google/api_client/client_secrets'
require 'google/api_client/auth/file_storage'
require 'google/api_client/auth/installed_app'

# This OAuth 2.0 access scope allows for read-only access to the authenticated
# user's account, but not other types of account access.
YOUTUBE_READONLY_SCOPE = 'https://www.googleapis.com/auth/youtube.readonly'
YOUTUBE_API_SERVICE_NAME = 'youtube'
YOUTUBE_API_VERSION = 'v3'

def get_authenticated_service
  client = Google::APIClient.new(
    :application_name => $PROGRAM_NAME,
    :application_version => '1.0.0'
  )
  youtube = client.discovered_api(YOUTUBE_API_SERVICE_NAME, YOUTUBE_API_VERSION)

  file_storage = Google::APIClient::FileStorage.new("#{$PROGRAM_NAME}-oauth2.json")
  if file_storage.authorization.nil?
    client_secrets = Google::APIClient::ClientSecrets.load
    flow = Google::APIClient::InstalledAppFlow.new(
      :client_id => client_secrets.client_id,
      :client_secret => client_secrets.client_secret,
      :scope => [YOUTUBE_READONLY_SCOPE]
    )
    client.authorization = flow.authorize(file_storage)
  else
    client.authorization = file_storage.authorization
  end

  return client, youtube
end

def main
  client, youtube = get_authenticated_service

  begin
    # Retrieve the "contentDetails" part of the channel resource for the
    # authenticated user's channel.
    channels_response = client.execute!(
      :api_method => youtube.channels.list,
      :parameters => {
        :mine => true,
        :part => 'contentDetails'
      }
    )

    channels_response.data.items.each do |channel|
      # From the API response, extract the playlist ID that identifies the list
      # of videos uploaded to the authenticated user's channel.
      uploads_list_id = channel['contentDetails']['relatedPlaylists']['uploads']

      # Retrieve the list of videos uploaded to the authenticated user's channel.
      next_page_token = ''
      until next_page_token.nil?
        playlistitems_response = client.execute!(
          :api_method => youtube.playlist_items.list,
          :parameters => {
            :playlistId => uploads_list_id,
            :part => 'snippet',
            :maxResults => 50,
            :pageToken => next_page_token
          }
        )

        puts "Videos in list #{uploads_list_id}"

        # Print information about each video.
        playlistitems_response.data.items.each do |playlist_item|
          title = playlist_item['snippet']['title']
          video_id = playlist_item['snippet']['resourceId']['videoId']

          puts "#{title} (#{video_id})"
        end

        next_page_token = playlistitems_response.next_page_token
      end

      puts
    end
  rescue Google::APIClient::TransmissionError => e
    puts e.result.body
  end
end

main

```

### Node.js Code Samples for YouTube API

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=th

Node.js code samples are now available through the interactive code snippet tool and in the documentation for most API methods, such as channels.list. These samples provide a starting point for Node.js applications and include utility functions like removeEmptyParameters.

```javascript
function removeEmptyParameters(params) {
  const newParams = {};
  for (const key in params) {
    if (params.hasOwnProperty(key) && params[key] !== null && params[key] !== '') {
      newParams[key] = params[key];
    }
  }
  return newParams;
}

// Example usage:
// const requestParams = {
//   part: 'snippet',
//   id: 'UCxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx',
//   maxResults: '' // This parameter would be removed by the function
// };
// const cleanedParams = removeEmptyParameters(requestParams);
// console.log(cleanedParams); // { part: 'snippet', id: 'UCxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx' }
```

### guideCategories.list

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=vi

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/guideCategories

### Description
Retrieves a list of YouTube guide categories.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/guideCategories

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **id** (string) - Required - The ID of the guide category to retrieve.

### Error Handling
#### Errors
- **notFound**: The guide category identified by the `id` parameter cannot be found.
  - **reason**: `notFound`
  - **cause**: The guide category identified by the `id` parameter cannot be found. Use the `guideCategories.list` method to retrieve a list of valid values.

### Response

- **items** (array) - A list of guide categories.

### GET /youtube/v3/search - search.list Updates

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=th

Updates to the `search.list` method include clarifications on the `order` parameter for live broadcasts sorted by `viewCount` and the supported parameters when `relatedToVideoId` is set.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/search - search.list

### Description
Retrieves a collection of search results that match the specified query (according to the API's search parameters).

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/youtube/v3/search`

### Query Parameters
- **order** (string) - Optional - Note: If you sort live broadcasts by `viewCount`, the API results are sorted by the broadcasts' number of concurrent viewers while the broadcasts are still ongoing.
- **relatedToVideoId** (string) - Optional - Returns the videos that are related to the video specified by this parameter. Note: If this parameter is set, the only other supported parameters are `part`, `maxResults`, `pageToken`, `regionCode`, `relevanceLanguage`, `safeSearch`, `type` (which must be set to `video`), and `fields`.
```

from googleapiclient.discovery import build


def insert_channel_banner(youtube, channel_id, image_path):
    """Inserts a channel banner using the YouTube Data API v3.

    Args:
        youtube: Authorized YouTube API service instance.
        channel_id: The ID of the channel to update.
        image_path: The path to the image file to upload as a banner.
    """
    try:
        request = youtube.channelBanners().insert(channelId=channel_id, body={})
        # This method typically requires multipart upload, handling depends on client library.
        # The actual upload logic would be more involved, including file handling.
        print(f"Initiating channel banner upload for channel {channel_id}.")
        # response = request.execute()
        # print(f"Channel banner updated successfully: {response}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"An error occurred: {e}")

if __name__ == '__main__':
    # Placeholder for authenticated YouTube API service
    # youtube = build('youtube', 'v3', credentials=credentials)

### Channel Banners, Channels Update, and Videos Methods - `onBehalfOfContentOwner` Parameter

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=tr

Information on the added support for the `onBehalfOfContentOwner` parameter in several channel and video related methods.

```APIDOC
## Channel and Video Methods - `onBehalfOfContentOwner` Parameter

### Description
The `onBehalfOfContentOwner` parameter is now supported by `channelBanners.insert`, `channels.update`, `videos.getRating`, and `videos.rate` methods. This parameter allows the authenticated user to act on behalf of a specified content owner.

### Supported Methods
- `channelBanners.insert`
- `channels.update`
- `videos.getRating`
- `videos.rate`

### Query Parameters
- **`onBehalfOfContentOwner`** (string) - Optional - Indicates that the authenticated user is acting on behalf of the content owner specified in the parameter value.
```

### GET /youtube/v3/playlistItems

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=vi

Retrieves playlist items, including status information like privacy status.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/playlistItems

### Description
Retrieves a collection of playlist items. The `status` object can be included, which contains the `privacyStatus` of the playlist item.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/playlistItems

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - Specifies the `playlistItem` resource parts that the API response will include. Comma-separated list. Can include `status`.
- **playlistId** (string) - Optional - The ID of the playlist for which to retrieve items.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "part": "snippet,status",
  "playlistId": "PLAYLIST_ID"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200 OK)
- **items** (array) - A list of playlist item resources.
  - **status** (object) - Status information about the playlist item.
    - **privacyStatus** (string) - The privacy status of the playlist item (e.g., 'public', 'private', 'unlisted').

#### Error Response
- **errors** (array) - Description of the error encountered.
```

```APIDOC
## Subscriptions List Parameters

### Description
The `subscriptions.list` method in the YouTube Data API v3 now supports the `onBehalfOfContentOwner` and `onBehalfOfContentOwnerChannel` parameters, which are also available for other methods.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/subscriptions`

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
N/A

#### Query Parameters
- **onBehalfOfContentOwner** (string) - Optional. The content owner's ID to use when acting on behalf of the content owner.
- **onBehalfOfContentOwnerChannel** (string) - Optional. The channel ID to use when acting on behalf of the content owner.

### Request Example
```
GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/subscriptions?part=snippet&onBehalfOfContentOwner=YOUR_CONTENT_OWNER_ID&onBehalfOfContentOwnerChannel=YOUR_CHANNEL_ID
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **kind** (string) - Identifies this as a collection of subscription resources.
- **etag** (string) - The ETag of the entire response.
- **nextPageToken** (string) - The token that can be used to retrieve the next page of results.
- **pageInfo** (object) - Paging details for the results.
- **items** (array) - A list of subscription resources.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "kind": "youtube#subscriptionListResponse",
  "etag": "YOUR_ETAG",
  "pageInfo": {
    "totalResults": 100,
    "resultsPerPage": 5
  },
  "items": [
    {
      "kind": "youtube#subscription",
      "etag": "YOUR_ETAG",
      "id": "YOUR_SUBSCRIPTION_ID",
      "snippet": {
        "publishedAt": "2023-01-01T00:00:00Z",
        "title": "Channel Title",
        "resourceId": {
          "kind": "youtube#channel",
          "channelId": "CHANNEL_ID"
        }
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

### JavaScript Example for Uploading a Video with YouTube Data API v3

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-cn

This snippet demonstrates how to upload a video using the YouTube Data API v3 with client-side JavaScript. It leverages the 'videos.insert' method and requires appropriate authentication and CORS configuration. This is an alternative to browser-based uploading in the v2 API.

```javascript
function uploadVideo(file, title, description, tags) {
  const uploadUrl = 'https://www.googleapis.com/upload/youtube/v3/videos?part=snippet,status&key=YOUR_API_KEY';

  const metadata = {
    snippet: {
      title: title,
      description: description,
      tags: tags
    },
    status: {
      privacyStatus: 'private' // or 'public', 'unlisted'
    }
  };

  const formData = new FormData();
  formData.append('metadata', new Blob([JSON.stringify(metadata)], { type: 'application/json' }));
  formData.append('file', file);

  return fetch(uploadUrl, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: {
      'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN
    },
    body: formData
  })
  .then(response => response.json())
  .then(data => {
    console.log('Video uploaded successfully:', data);
    return data;
  })
  .catch(error => {
    console.error('Error uploading video:', error);
    throw error;
  });
}

// Example usage:
// const fileInput = document.getElementById('fileInput');
// const titleInput = document.getElementById('titleInput');
// const descriptionInput = document.getElementById('descriptionInput');
// const tagsInput = document.getElementById('tagsInput');

// fileInput.addEventListener('change', (event) => {
//   const file = event.target.files[0];
//   const title = titleInput.value;
//   const description = descriptionInput.value;
//   const tags = tagsInput.value.split(',');
//   uploadVideo(file, title, description, tags);
// });
```

### GET /youtube/v3/playlistImages

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/docs/playlistImages/list

Retrieves playlist images based on provided parameters. Requires authorization and specifies which parts of the playlist image resource to return.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/playlistImages

### Description
Retrieves a collection of playlist images associated with a specific playlist or image ID. This endpoint requires authentication and is subject to quota limitations.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/youtube/v3/playlistImages`

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - Comma-separated list of playlist image resource properties that the API response will include. Valid values include `snippet`.
- **playlistId** (string) - Required (if `id` is not specified) - The ID of the playlist for which the images should be retrieved.
- **id** (string) - Required (if `playlistId` is not specified) - The ID of the playlist image.
- **maxResults** (integer) - Optional - The maximum number of results to return. Maximum value is 50.
- **pageToken** (string) - Optional - The token for fetching the next page of images.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "example": "GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/playlistImages?part=snippet&playlistId=PL_z_8CaFkkyjS7C7_h-zQ43jJj_f4i-t7&maxResults=5"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **kind** (string) - Identifies the API resource's type. The value will be `youtube#playlistImageListResponse`.
- **nextPageToken** (string) - The token that can be used as the value of the `pageToken` parameter to retrieve the next page in the result set.
- **prevPageToken** (string) - The token that can be used as the value of the `pageToken` parameter to retrieve the previous page in the result set.
- **pageInfo** (object) - Encapsulates paging information for the result set.
  - **totalResults** (integer) - The total number of results in the result set.
  - **resultsPerPage** (integer) - The number of results included in the API response.
- **items** (list) - A list of playlist images that match the request criteria.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "kind": "youtube#playlistImageListResponse",
  "pageInfo": {
    "totalResults": 100,
    "resultsPerPage": 5
  },
  "items": [
    {
      "kind": "youtube#playlistImage",
      "etag": "...",
      "id": "...",
      "snippet": {
        "title": "Playlist Title",
        "description": "Playlist Description",
        "publishedAt": "2023-01-01T10:00:00Z",
        "channelId": "..."
      }
    }
  ]
}
```
```
