### GET /search (eventType parameter)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=vi

The `search.list` method now supports the `eventType` parameter to filter broadcast events.

```APIDOC
## GET /search with eventType Parameter

### Description
This endpoint searches for resources that match the specified query. The `eventType` parameter allows you to filter search results to include only active, upcoming, or completed broadcast events.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/search`

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
None

#### Query Parameters
* **eventType** (string) - Optional. Filters broadcast events. Valid values are `completed`, `live`, or `upcoming`.
* **q** (string) - Required. The search query.
* **type** (string) - Required. The type of resource to search for (e.g., `video`, `channel`, `playlist`).

#### Request Body
None

### Request Example
```
GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/search?q=google+io&eventType=upcoming&type=video&key=YOUR_API_KEY
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
* **items** (array) - An array of search results.
  * Each item contains details about the found resource (e.g., video, channel, playlist).

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "items": [
    {
      "kind": "youtube#searchResult",
      "etag": "...",
      "id": {
        "kind": "youtube#video",
        "videoId": "..."
      },
      "snippet": {
        "publishedAt": "2023-05-10T08:00:00Z",
        "channelId": "...",
        "title": "Google I/O 2023 Keynote",
        "description": "...",
        "thumbnails": {
          "default": {"url": "..."},
          "medium": {"url": "..."},
          "high": {"url": "..."}
        },
        "liveBroadcastContent": "upcoming"
      }
    }
  ]
}
```
```

### Insert Activities - Go

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=th

Provides a Go code sample for inserting activities using the YouTube Data API v3. This snippet demonstrates how to authenticate and make the API call.

```Go
package main

import (
	"context"
	"fmt"
	"log"

	"google.golang.org/api/option"
	"google.golang.org/api/youtube/v3"
)

func main() {
	ctx := context.Background()

	service, err := youtube.NewService(ctx, option.WithAPIKey("YOUR_API_KEY"))
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Unable to create YouTube service: %v", err)
	}

	activity := &youtube.Activity{
		Snippet: &youtube.ActivitySnippet{
			Title:       "My Awesome Activity",
			Description: "This is a description for my awesome activity.",
		},
		ContentDetails: &youtube.ActivityContentDetails{
			// Add content details here, e.g., related to playlists or videos
		},
	}

	_, err = service.Activities.Insert([]string{"snippet", "contentDetails"}, activity).Context(ctx).Do()
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Error inserting activity: %v", err)
	}

	fmt.Println("Activity inserted successfully!")
}

```

### GET /youtube/v3/search - Updates to order parameter

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=tr

Updates to the `search.list` method's `order` parameter. Sorting live broadcasts by `viewCount` now sorts by concurrent viewers while ongoing.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/search

### Description
Updates to the `search.list` method's `order` parameter. If you sort live broadcasts by `viewCount`, the API results are sorted by the broadcasts' number of concurrent viewers while the broadcasts are still ongoing.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/search

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **order** (string) - Optional - Specifies the order in which the results are returned. If sorting live broadcasts by `viewCount`, results are sorted by concurrent viewers.
```

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/videos

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/videos

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **id** (string) - Required - The ID of the video to retrieve.

### Response
#### Error Response (404)
- **error.code** (integer) - The HTTP status code of the error.
- **error.message** (string) - A message that identifies the error.
- **error.errors** (array) - The reason for the error.
  - **error.errors.reason** (string) - The specific reason for the error, e.g., `videoNotFound`.

#### Response Example
{
  "error": {
    "code": 404,
    "message": "Video not found.",
    "errors": [
      {
        "reason": "videoNotFound"
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

### videos.insert, videos.update, videos.delete - onBehalfOfContentOwner Parameter

```APIDOC
## Videos API - Content Owner Management

### Description
The `onBehalfOfContentOwner` parameter is now supported for `videos.insert`, `videos.update`, and `videos.delete` methods. This allows authenticated YouTube CMS users to act on behalf of a specified content owner, managing videos across multiple channels.

POST, PUT, DELETE

    },
    "status": {
      "privacyStatus": "public"
    }
  },
  "onBehalfOfContentOwner": "YOUR_CONTENT_OWNER_ID",

}

### GET /search - eventType Parameter

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=tr

The `search.list` method now supports the `eventType` parameter to filter broadcast events.

```APIDOC
## GET /search

### Description
Searches for resources that match the specified query. Supports the `eventType` parameter to filter broadcast events.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/youtube/v3/search`

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
N/A

#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - The `part` parameter specifies the search resource parts that the API response includes. Valid values are `id` and `snippet`.
- **eventType** (string) - Optional - Restricts search results to only broadcast events of the specified type. Valid values are `completed`, `live`, `upcoming`.
- **q** (string) - Required - The query term to search for.

#### Request Body
N/A

### Request Example
```
GET /youtube/v3/search?part=snippet&q=Google+IO+2016&eventType=upcoming HTTP/1.1
Host: www.googleapis.com
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **kind** (string) - The type of the API resource.
- **etag** (string) - The ETag of the response.
- **items** (array) - A list of search results.
  - **kind** (string) - The type of the search result.
  - **etag** (string) - The ETag of the search result.
  - **id** (object) - The ID object for the search result.
    - **kind** (string) - The type of the resource ID.
    - **videoId** (string) - The video ID.
  - **snippet** (object) - The snippet object for the search result.
    - **title** (string) - The title of the search result.
    - **publishedAt** (string) - The date and time when the video was published.
    - **channelId** (string) - The ID of the channel that published the video.
    - **liveBroadcastContent** (string) - Indicates live broadcast status (e.g., `upcoming`, `active`, `none`).

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "kind": "youtube#searchListResponse",
  "etag": "...",
  "items": [
    {
      "kind": "youtube#searchResult",
      "etag": "...",
      "id": {
        "kind": "youtube#video",
        "videoId": "VIDEO_ID"
      },
      "snippet": {
        "publishedAt": "2016-05-11T10:00:00Z",
        "channelId": "UC...",
        "title": "Google I/O 2016 Keynote",
        "description": "The Google I/O 2016 Keynote.",
        "liveBroadcastContent": "completed"
      }
    }
  ]
}
```
```

### GET /videos

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=th

Retrieves a list of videos. Supports filtering by `myRating` and pagination. The `myRating` parameter enables you to retrieve a list of videos that the authenticated user rated with a `like` or `dislike` rating.

```APIDOC
## GET /videos

### Description
Retrieves a list of videos. Supports filtering by `myRating` and pagination. The `myRating` parameter enables you to retrieve a list of videos that the authenticated user rated with a `like` or `dislike` rating. Note that paging parameters are only supported for requests using the `myRating` parameter.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/videos

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - Comma-separated list of channel resource parts to retrieve.
- **myRating** (string) - Optional - Filter videos based on the authenticated user's rating (`like` or `dislike`).
- **id** (string) - Optional - Filter videos based on video ID. If `id` is used, `myRating` cannot be used.
- **maxResults** (integer) - Optional - The maximum number of videos that the API can return in the result set. Defaults to 5, maximum is 50.
- **pageToken** (string) - Optional - The token that identifies a specific page in the result set.

### Request Example
```
GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/videos?part=snippet&myRating=like&maxResults=10&pageToken=PAGE_TOKEN
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **kind** (string) - The type of the API response.
- **etag** (string) - The ETag of the response.
- **items** (array) - An array of video resources.
  - **kind** (string) - The type of the resource.
  - **etag** (string) - The ETag of the resource.
  - **id** (string) - The ID of the video.
  - **snippet** (object) - The snippet of the video.
- **pageInfo** (object) - Contains details about the pagination of the result set.
  - **totalResults** (integer) - The total number of results available.
  - **resultsPerPage** (integer) - The number of results included in the current result set.
- **nextPageToken** (string) - A token that can be used to retrieve the next page of results.
- **prevPageToken** (string) - A token that can be used to retrieve the previous page of results.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "kind": "youtube#videoListResponse",
  "etag": "ETAG_VALUE",
  "items": [
    {
      "kind": "youtube#video",
      "etag": "ETAG_VALUE",
      "id": "VIDEO_ID1",
      "snippet": {
        "publishedAt": "2023-01-01T12:00:00Z",
        "channelId": "CHANNEL_ID",
        "title": "Video Title 1",
        "description": "Video description 1",
        "thumbnails": {},
        "channelTitle": "Channel Title",
        "tags": ["tag1", "tag2"]
      }
    },
    {
      "kind": "youtube#video",
      "etag": "ETAG_VALUE",
      "id": "VIDEO_ID2",
      "snippet": {
        "publishedAt": "2023-01-02T12:00:00Z",
        "channelId": "CHANNEL_ID",
        "title": "Video Title 2",
        "description": "Video description 2",
        "thumbnails": {},
        "channelTitle": "Channel Title",
        "tags": ["tag3", "tag4"]
      }
    }
  ],
  "pageInfo": {
    "totalResults": 20,
    "resultsPerPage": 2
  },
  "nextPageToken": "NEXT_PAGE_TOKEN_VALUE",
  "prevPageToken": "PREV_PAGE_TOKEN_VALUE"
}
```

### Error Handling
- **403 Forbidden**: Returned for requests that attempt to retrieve video rating information but are not properly authorized.
```

### Handling Approximate Total Results in Search (YouTube Data API v3)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=tr

This example shows how to manage the 'pageInfo.totalResults' property returned by the search.list method. It highlights that the value is an approximation, capped at 1,000,000, and advises against using it for pagination, instead recommending 'nextPageToken' and 'prevPageToken'.

```javascript
function handleSearchResults(response) {
  const totalResults = response.pageInfo.totalResults;
  const nextPageToken = response.nextPageToken;
  const prevPageToken = response.prevPageToken;

  console.log(`Approximate total results: ${totalResults}`);

  if (nextPageToken) {
    console.log('Show next page button');
  }
  if (prevPageToken) {
    console.log('Show previous page button');
  }
}
```

### YouTube Data API v3 - Optimizing Performance (ETags and gzip)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/getting-started

This section covers performance optimization techniques for the YouTube Data API v3, focusing on the use of ETags for caching and gzip compression for bandwidth reduction.

```APIDOC
## Optimizing Performance

### Description
To enhance the efficiency of your API interactions, the YouTube Data API v3 supports several performance optimization techniques, including the use of ETags for caching and gzip compression for reducing bandwidth.

### Using ETags
*   **Purpose**: ETags (Entity Tags) are HTTP response headers that allow clients to determine if a resource has changed since the last request. This is crucial for efficient caching and preventing unnecessary data transfer.
*   **How it works**:
    1.  When you request a resource, the API response includes an `ETag` header.
    2.  You store this ETag along with the cached resource.
    3.  For subsequent requests, you include the stored ETag in the `If-None-Match` request header.
    4.  If the resource has not changed, the API returns a `304 Not Modified` status code with an empty body, saving bandwidth.
    5.  If the resource has changed, the API returns the updated resource with a new `ETag`.
*   **Example Request Header**:
    ```
    If-None-Match: "some_etag_value"
    ```

### Using gzip Compression
*   **Purpose**: gzip compression reduces the size of API responses, leading to faster download times and lower bandwidth consumption.
*   **How it works**:
    1.  Include the `Accept-Encoding: gzip` header in your API requests.
    2.  If the server supports it and the response can be compressed, the API will return a gzipped response with the `Content-Encoding: gzip` header.
    3.  Your client library or application needs to be able to decompress the gzipped content.
*   **Example Request Header**:
    ```
    Accept-Encoding: gzip
    ```

### Benefits
*   **Reduced Latency**: Faster retrieval of data due to efficient caching and smaller payloads.
*   **Lower Bandwidth Costs**: Significant savings on data transfer costs for both the developer and the end-user.
*   **Improved User Experience**: Applications feel more responsive and perform better.
```

```APIDOC
## GET /channels

### Description
Retrieves a list of channels. This endpoint can be used to fetch information about one or more channels based on their IDs.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/channels

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - The part parameter specifies the channel resources that the API response should include. Valid values are id, snippet, contentDetails, statistics, topicDetails.
- **id** (string) - Optional - The id parameter specifies the unique ID of the channel to retrieve. 

### Request Example
```json
{
  "example": "GET /youtube/v3/channels?part=snippet&id=UC_x5XG1OV2P6uZZ5FSM9Ttw"

```

#### Response Example

  "example": {
    "kind": "youtube#channelListResponse",
    "etag": "...",
    "items": [
      {
        "kind": "youtube#channel",
        "etag": "...",
        "id": "UC_x5XG1OV2P6uZZ5FSM9Ttw",
        "snippet": {
          "title": "YouTube Developers",

### YouTube API: Uploading Videos with Error Handling (Java)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-tw

Illustrates how to use the `videos.insert` method in Java, including handling potential `badRequest` errors such as `invalidCategoryId`, `invalidRecordingDetails`, `invalidVideoGameRating`, and `invalidVideoMetadata`. It requires proper setup of the YouTube API client and authentication.

```java
import com.google.api.client.googleapis.json.GoogleJsonResponseException;
import com.google.api.services.youtube.YouTube;
import com.google.api.services.youtube.model.Video;
import com.google.api.services.youtube.model.VideoSnippet;

// ... (YouTube API client initialization and authentication)

YouTube youtube = ...; // Initialize YouTube client

Video video = new Video();
VideoSnippet snippet = new VideoSnippet();
// Set snippet properties, e.g., snippet.setCategoryId("20");
video.setSnippet(snippet);

try {
    YouTube.Videos.Insert insertRequest = youtube.videos().insert("snippet,status", video);
    // Execute the request and handle the response
    // insertRequest.execute();
} catch (GoogleJsonResponseException e) {
    if (e.getDetails().getErrors() != null) {
        for (com.google.api.client.googleapis.json.GoogleJsonResponseException.ErrorInfo errorInfo : e.getDetails().getErrors()) {
            if (errorInfo.getReason().equals("invalidCategoryId")) {
                System.err.println("Error: Invalid category ID.");
            } else if (errorInfo.getReason().equals("invalidRecordingDetails")) {
                System.err.println("Error: Invalid recording details.");
            } // ... handle other error reasons
        }
    }
} catch (Exception e) {
    e.printStackTrace();
}

```

### Enable Gzip Compression in HTTP Headers

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/getting-started

To enable gzip compression for API responses, you need to set the 'Accept-Encoding' header to 'gzip' and modify your user agent string to include 'gzip'. This reduces bandwidth consumption at the cost of increased CPU usage for decompression.

```http
Accept-Encoding: gzip
User-Agent: my program (gzip)
```

### Get Authenticated User's Uploads

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/channels

### Description
Retrieves the 'contentDetails' part of the channel resource for the authenticated user's channel to obtain the 'uploads' playlist ID.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/channels

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **mine** (boolean) - Required - Set to true to retrieve the channel of the authenticated user.
- **part** (string) - Required - Specifies the parts of the channel resource to retrieve. Use 'contentDetails' to get playlist IDs.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "parameters": {
    "mine": true,
    "part": "contentDetails"
  }
}
```

### Response

- **items** (array) - A list of channel resources. For the authenticated user, this will contain one channel.
  - **contentDetails** (object)
    - **relatedPlaylists** (object)
      - **uploads** (string) - The ID of the playlist that contains the channel's uploaded videos.

#### Response Example

  "items": [
    {
      "contentDetails": {
        "relatedPlaylists": {
          "uploads": "UUxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx"
        }
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

## GET /youtube/v3/playlistItems

### Description
Retrieves a list of videos from a specified playlist, such as the uploads playlist of a channel. It supports pagination to retrieve all items.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/playlistItems

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **playlistId** (string) - Required - The ID of the playlist to retrieve items from.
- **part** (string) - Required - Specifies the parts of the playlist item resource to retrieve. Use 'snippet' to get video details.
- **maxResults** (integer) - Optional - The maximum number of results to return. Maximum is 50.
- **pageToken** (string) - Optional - The token for the next page of results.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "parameters": {
    "playlistId": "UUxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx",
    "part": "snippet",
    "maxResults": 50,
    "pageToken": ""
  }
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **items** (array) - A list of playlist items.
  - **snippet** (object)
    - **title** (string) - The title of the video.
    - **resourceId** (object)
      - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the video.
- **nextPageToken** (string) - The token that can be used to retrieve the next page of results.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "items": [
    {
      "snippet": {
        "title": "Example Video Title",
        "resourceId": {
          "videoId": "dQw4w9WgXcQ"
        }
      }
    }
  ],
  "nextPageToken": "CAUQAA"
}
```
```

### Optimizing Performance with gzip Compression

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/getting-started

Enable gzip compression to reduce the bandwidth required for API responses, although it will increase CPU usage for decompression.

```APIDOC
## Optimizing Performance with gzip Compression

### Description
Enabling gzip compression for API responses can significantly reduce bandwidth consumption. While this requires additional CPU time for decompression, the network resource savings often outweigh the cost.

### Requirements
To receive a gzip-encoded response, you must:
1.  Set the `Accept-Encoding` HTTP request header to `gzip`.
2.  Modify your User-Agent string to include the substring `gzip`.

### Sample HTTP Headers
```
Accept-Encoding: gzip
User-Agent: my program (gzip)
```
```

### Node.js Code Samples for YouTube API v3

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-cn

Interactive Node.js code samples are now available for the YouTube API v3. These samples provide a starting point for Node.js applications and include utility functions like 'removeEmptyParameters' for cleaning API request parameters. They are accessible via the API method documentation.

```javascript
function removeEmptyParameters(params) {
  const newParams = {};
  for (const key in params) {
    if (params.hasOwnProperty(key) && params[key]) {
      newParams[key] = params[key];
    }
  }
  return newParams;
}
```

### YouTube API: Insert Video (Go)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=vi

Demonstrates how to upload a new video using the YouTube Data API v3 in Go. This includes setting video details and metadata.

```Go
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"log"

	"google.golang.org/api/youtube/v3"
	"google.golang.org/api/googleapi"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
)

func main() {
	// Assume client is an authorized *http.Client
	sservice, err := youtube.New(client)
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Error creating YouTube client: %v", err)
	}

	video := &youtube.Video{
		Snippet: &youtube.VideoSnippet{
			Title:       "My Awesome Video",
			Description: "This is a description of my awesome video.",
			Tags:        []string{"go", "youtube", "api"},
			CategoryId:  "22", // Example category ID for 'People & Blogs'
		},
		Status: &youtube.VideoStatus{
			PrivacyStatus: "private", // or "public", "unlisted"
		},
	}

	filePath := "path/to/your/video.mp4" // Replace with actual video file path

	file, err := os.Open(filePath)
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Error opening video file: %v", err)
	}
	defer file.Close()

	// Create a GoogleAPI file object from the file handle
	fileInfo, err := file.Stat()
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Error getting file info: %v", err)
	}

	driveFile := &googleapi.Media{
		Name    : filepath.Base(filePath),
		Reader  : file,
		Length  : fileInfo.Size(),
		ContentType: "video/mp4", // Adjust content type if needed
	}

	call := service.Videos.Insert("snippet,status", video, driveFile)

	response, err := call.Do()
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Error making API call to insert video: %v", err)
	}

	fmt.Printf("Video uploaded successfully: %+v\n", response)
}

```

--------------------------------

### Python Authorization Flow with google-auth Libraries

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=vi

This Python code sample demonstrates authorization flows using the google-auth and google-auth-oauthlib libraries, replacing the deprecated oauth2client library. It supports both installed applications and web server applications with different authorization strategies.

```Python
from google_auth_oauthlib.flow import InstalledAppFlow

# For installed applications:
flow = InstalledAppFlow.from_client_secrets_file(
    'client_secrets.json', scopes=['https://www.googleapis.com/auth/youtube.force-ssl'])
credentials = flow.run_local_server(port=0)

# For web server applications (using Flask as an example):
# from flask import Flask, redirect, url_for
# import google_auth_oauthlib.flow
# app = Flask(__name__)
# flow = google_auth_oauthlib.flow.Flow.from_client_secrets_file(
#     'client_secrets.json',
#     scopes=['https://www.googleapis.com/auth/youtube.force-ssl'],
#     redirect_uri=url_for('oauth2callback', _external=True))
# authorization_url, state = flow.authorization_url(
#     access_type='offline',
#     prompt='consent')
# return redirect(authorization_url)
```

### GET /search

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-tw

The search endpoint allows you to search for YouTube videos, channels, and playlists. You can filter results by various criteria.

```APIDOC
## GET /search

### Description
The search endpoint allows you to search for YouTube videos, channels, and playlists. You can filter results by various criteria.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/search

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - The part parameter specifies the search resource types that the API response should include. Valid values are id, snippet.
- **q** (string) - Required - The query term to search for.
- **type** (string) - Optional - The type parameter restricts the search to a specific resource type. Valid values are channel, playlist, video.
- **forContentOwner** (boolean) - Optional - This parameter can only be used in a properly authorized request. Set to true to also search
  for resources that the content owner has access to.
- **regionCode** (string) - Optional - The regionCode parameter restricts search results to videos that can be viewed in the specified region.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "example": "GET /youtube/v3/search?part=snippet&q=google+developers&type=video"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **items** (array) - An array of search result resources.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "example": {
    "kind": "youtube#searchListResponse",
    "etag": "...",
    "items": [
      {
        "kind": "youtube#searchResult",
        "etag": "...",
        "id": {
          "kind": "youtube#video",
          "videoId": "dQw4w9WgXcQ"
        },
        "snippet": {
          "title": "Rick Astley - Never Gonna Give You Up (Official Music Video)",
          "description": "...",
          "thumbnails": {
            "default": {"url": "..."},
            "medium": {"url": "..."},
            "high": {"url": "..."}
          },
          "channelTitle": "Rick Astley"
        }
      }
    ]
  }
}
```
```

### GET /youtube/v3/videos

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=th

Retrieves information about YouTube videos, with support for specifying maximum dimensions for embedded players.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/videos

### Description
Retrieves information about YouTube videos. This endpoint supports new parameters `maxHeight` and `maxWidth` to control the dimensions of the embedded player returned in the `player.embedHtml` property.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/videos

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **maxHeight** (integer) - Optional - Specifies the maximum height of the embedded player.
- **maxWidth** (integer) - Optional - Specifies the maximum width of the embedded player.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "example": "GET /youtube/v3/videos?part=player&id=VIDEO_ID&maxHeight=720&maxWidth=1280"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **player.embedHtml** (string) - An iframe tag for embedding the video player.
- **player.embedHeight** (integer) - The height of the embedded player.
- **player.embedWidth** (integer) - The width of the embedded player.
- **contentDetails.hasCustomThumbnail** (boolean) - Indicates if the video uploader provided a custom thumbnail (visible only to the uploader).
- **contentDetails.contentRating.fpbRatingReasons[]** (string) - Reasons for the video's FPB (South Africa) rating.
- **contentDetails.contentRating.mcstRating** (string) - The video's rating in Vietnam.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "example": "{\n  \"items\": [\n    {\n      \"player\": {\n        \"embedHtml\": \"<iframe width=\"1280\" height=\"720\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/VIDEO_ID\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen></iframe>\",\n        \"embedHeight\": 720,\n        \"embedWidth\": 1280\n      },\n      \"contentDetails\": {\n        \"hasCustomThumbnail\": true,\n        \"contentRating\": {\n          \"fpbRatingReasons\": [\n            \"violence\"\n          ],\n          \"mcstRating\": \"G\"\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  ]\n}"
}
```
```

### Videos API - Get Rating

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-cn

The videos.getRating method retrieves the ratings that the authenticated user gave to a list of one or more videos.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/videos/getRating

### Description
Retrieves the ratings that the authenticated user gave to a list of one or more videos.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/videos/getRating

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **id** (string) - Required - A comma-separated list of video IDs for which to retrieve ratings. Maximum of 50 IDs.

### Request Example
GET /youtube/v3/videos/getRating?id=VIDEO_ID_1,VIDEO_ID_2

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **items** (array) - A list of ratings for the requested videos.
  - **rating** (string) - The rating given by the authenticated user ('like' or 'dislike').

#### Response Example
{
  "kind": "youtube#videoListResponse",
  "etag": "...",
  "items": [
    {
      "id": "VIDEO_ID_1",
      "rating": "like"
    },
    {
      "id": "VIDEO_ID_2",
      "rating": "dislike"
    }
  ]
}

#### Error Response (403)
- **forbidden** (string) - Returned for requests that attempt to retrieve video rating information but are not properly authorized.

```

### Endpoint
/videos/rate

### Insert Caption Track with Timing Info (YouTube Data API v3)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=th

Following the deprecation of the 'sync' parameter, this example shows how to insert a caption track by providing the necessary timing information. This is crucial for ensuring successful uploads of caption tracks.

```json
{
  "kind": "youtube#caption",
  "snippet": {
    "videoId": "VIDEO_ID",
    "language": "en",
    "name": "English Captions",
    "trackInfo": {
      "timing": {
        "format": "SRT",
        "data": "1\n00:00:01,000 --> 00:00:03,000\nHello world"
      }
    }
  }
}
```

### YouTube Data API v3 - Release Notes (March 11, 2015)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=vi

Details changes introduced on March 11, 2015, including updates to the migration guide and specific feature support or deprecation in the v3 API.

```APIDOC
## March 11, 2015 Release Notes

This update contains the following changes:

### Migration Guide Updates

*   **New Tab Added**: The YouTube Data API (v3) migration guide now includes a "New in the v3 API" tab listing features supported in v3 but not in v2.
*   **v2 Feature Support Noted**: The migration guide indicates that the v3 API will support the "Flagging a video" feature from the v2 API.
*   **v2 Features Not Supported in v3**: The migration guide has been updated to list v2 API features that will *not* be supported in the v3 API:
    *   Retrieve video recommendations (v3 alternative: `activities.list` with `home=true`, checking `snippet.type == 'recommendation'`)
    *   Retrieve channel suggestions
    *   Retrieve new subscription videos (v3 alternative: `activities.list` with `home=true`, checking `snippet.type == 'upload'`)
    *   RSS feed support
    *   Push notifications for feed updates (v3 supports PubSubHubbub for video uploads and updates to titles/descriptions only).

### Scope Update

*   A new scope is required for calls to all methods of the `caption` resource.
```

--------------------------------

### I18nRegions: list

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/docs/i18nRegions/list

Returns a list of content regions that the YouTube website supports. This method has a quota cost of 1 unit.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/i18nRegions

### Description
Returns a list of content regions that the YouTube website supports.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/i18nRegions

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - Specifies the `i18nRegion` resource properties that the API response will include. Set the parameter value to `snippet`.
- **hl** (string) - Optional - Specifies the language that should be used for text values in the API response. The default value is `en_US`.

### Request Body
Do not provide a request body when calling this method.

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **kind** (string) - Identifies the API resource's type. The value will be `youtube#i18nRegionListResponse`.
- **etag** (etag) - The Etag of this resource.
- **items[]** (list) - A list of regions where YouTube is available. In this map, the i18n region ID is the map key, and its value is the corresponding `i18nRegion` resource.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "kind": "youtube#i18nRegionListResponse",
  "etag": "etag",
  "items": [
    // i18nRegion resource objects
  ]
}
```

### Errors
This method could return general API errors listed in the error message documentation.
```

### OAuth 2.0 Authorization Flow in Go

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/code_samples/go

This Go code implements the OAuth 2.0 authorization flow for the YouTube Data API v3. It reads client secrets from 'client_secret.json', handles token retrieval either from a local cache or via a web server/prompt, and generates an authenticated HTTP client. It supports both web application and installed application flows.

```go
package main

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"io/ioutil"
	"log"
	"net"
	"net/http"
	"net/url"
	"os"
	"os/exec"
	"os/user"
	"path/filepath"
	"runtime"

	"golang.org/x/net/context"
	"golang.org/x/oauth2"
	"golang.org/x/oauth2/google"
)

// This variable indicates whether the script should launch a web server to
// initiate the authorization flow or just display the URL in the terminal
// window. Note the following instructions based on this setting:
// * launchWebServer = true
//   1. Use OAuth2 credentials for a web application
//   2. Define authorized redirect URIs for the credential in the Google APIs
//      Console and set the RedirectURL property on the config object to one
//      of those redirect URIs. For example:
//      config.RedirectURL = "http://localhost:8090"
//   3. In the startWebServer function below, update the URL in this line
//      to match the redirect URI you selected:
//         listener, err := net.Listen("tcp", "localhost:8090")
//      The redirect URI identifies the URI to which the user is sent after
//      completing the authorization flow. The listener then captures the
//      authorization code in the URL and passes it back to this script.
// * launchWebServer = false
//   1. Use OAuth2 credentials for an installed application. (When choosing
//      the application type for the OAuth2 client ID, select "Other".)
//   2. Set the redirect URI to "urn:ietf:wg:oauth:2.0:oob", like this:
//      config.RedirectURL = "urn:ietf:wg:oauth:2.0:oob"
//   3. When running the script, complete the auth flow. Then copy the
//      authorization code from the browser and enter it on the command line.
const launchWebServer = false

const missingClientSecretsMessage = `
		Please configure OAuth 2.0
		To make this sample run, you need to populate the client_secrets.json file
		found at:
		   %v
		with information from the {{ Google Cloud Console }}
		{{ https://cloud.google.com/console }}
		For more information about the client_secrets.json file format, please visit:
		https://developers.google.com/api-client-library/python/guide/aaa_client_secrets
		`

// getClient uses a Context and Config to retrieve a Token
// then generate a Client. It returns the generated Client.
func getClient(scope string) *http.Client {
	ctx := context.Background()
	
b, err := ioutil.ReadFile("client_secret.json")
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Unable to read client secret file: %v", err)
	}
	
	// If modifying the scope, delete your previously saved credentials
	// at ~/.credentials/youtube-go.json
	config, err := google.ConfigFromJSON(b, scope)
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Unable to parse client secret file to config: %v", err)
	}
	
	// Use a redirect URI like this for a web app. The redirect URI must be a
	// valid one for your OAuth2 credentials.
	config.RedirectURL = "http://localhost:8090"
	// Use the following redirect URI if launchWebServer=false in oauth2.go
	// config.RedirectURL = "urn:ietf:wg:oauth:2.0:oob"
	
	cacheFile, err := tokenCacheFile()
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Unable to get path to cached credential file. %v", err)
	}
	tok, err := tokenFromFile(cacheFile)
	if err != nil {
		authURL := config.AuthCodeURL("state-token", oauth2.AccessTypeOffline)
		if launchWebServer {
			fmt.Println("Trying to get token from web")
			tok, err = getTokenFromWeb(config, authURL)
		} else {
			fmt.Println("Trying to get token from prompt")
			tok, err = getTokenFromPrompt(config, authURL)
		}
		if err == nil {
			saveToken(cacheFile, tok)
		}
	}
	return config.Client(ctx, tok)
}

// startWebServer starts a web server that listens on http://localhost:8080.
// The webserver waits for an oauth code in the three-legged auth flow.
func startWebServer() (codeCh chan string, err error) {
	listener, err := net.Listen("tcp", "localhost:8090")
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	codeCh = make(chan string)

	go http.Serve(listener, http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
		code := r.FormValue("code")
		codeCh <- code // send code to OAuth flow
		listener.Close()
		w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "text/plain")
		fmt.Fprintf(w, "Received code: %v\r\nYou can now safely close this browser window.", code)
	}))

	return codeCh, nil
}

// openURL opens a browser window to the specified location.
// This code originally appeared at:
//   http://stackoverflow.com/questions/10377243/how-can-i-launch-a-process-that-is-not-a-file-in-go
func openURL(url string) error {
	var err error
	switch runtime.GOOS {
	case "linux":
		err = exec.Command("xdg-open", url).Start()
	case "windows":
		err = exec.Command("rundll32", "url.dll,FileProtocolHandler", "http://localhost:4001/").Start()
	case "darwin":

```

### videos.insert, videos.update, videos.delete - onBehalfOfContentOwner Parameter

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=th

The onBehalfOfContentOwner parameter is now supported for videos.insert, videos.update, and videos.delete methods. This allows YouTube CMS users to manage videos on behalf of a specified content owner.

```APIDOC
## Videos API - onBehalfOfContentOwner Parameter

### Description
The `onBehalfOfContentOwner` parameter enables authenticated YouTube CMS users to perform operations (insert, update, delete) on videos associated with a specified content owner. For `videos.insert`, `onBehalfOfContentOwnerChannel` must also be specified.

### Method
POST, PUT, DELETE

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/videos (insert, update, delete)

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters (for videos.delete)
- **id** (string) - Required - The ID of the video to delete.

#### Query Parameters
- **onBehalfOfContentOwner** (string) - Optional - Specifies the content owner on whose behalf the request is being made. The authenticated user's CMS account must be linked to this content owner.
- **onBehalfOfContentOwnerChannel** (string) - Required when using `onBehalfOfContentOwner` with `videos.insert` - Identifies the channel to which the video will be added.

### Request Example (videos.insert)
```json
{
  "example": "POST https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/videos?onBehalfOfContentOwner=CONTENT_OWNER_ID&onBehalfOfContentOwnerChannel=CHANNEL_ID&key={YOUR_API_KEY}&part=snippet,status\n{\n  \"snippet\": {\n    \"title\": \"New Video Title\",\n    \"description\": \"Video description.\",\n    \"tags\": [\n      \"tag1\",\n      \"tag2\"\n    ],\n    \"categoryId\": \"22\"\n  },\n  \"status\": {\n    \"privacyStatus\": \"public\"\n  }\n}"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **id** (string) - The ID of the created, updated, or deleted video.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "example": "{\n  \"kind\": \"youtube#video\",\n  \"etag\": \"...\",\n  \"id\": \"VIDEO_ID\"\n}"
}
```
```

### GET /youtube/v3/videos - Content Rating Systems Update

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-cn

This update expands the video resource to support 43 new content rating systems from various national rating agencies, allowing for more granular content classification.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/videos

### Description
This endpoint allows retrieval of video resources. The recent update expands support for content rating systems from numerous countries, enhancing the ability to categorize videos based on regional content standards.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/videos

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - Specifies the video resource parts you want to retrieve. Example: `snippet,contentDetails`
- **id** (string) - Optional - A comma-separated list of video IDs to retrieve.

#### Request Body
None

### Request Example
```bash
GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/videos?part=snippet,contentDetails&id=VIDEO_ID
```

### Response

- **items** (array) - A list of video resources matching the request.
  - **snippet** (object) - Contains details about the video.
    - **title** (string) - The title of the video.
  - **contentDetails** (object) - Contains details about the video's content.
    - **contentRating** (object) - Information about the video's content rating.
      - **incaaRating** (string) - Content rating for Argentina.

  "items": [

### videos.insert, videos.update, videos.delete - onBehalfOfContentOwner parameter

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-tw

The onBehalfOfContentOwner parameter is now supported for videos.insert, videos.update, and videos.delete methods, allowing content owners to manage videos across their channels.

```APIDOC
## videos.insert, videos.update, videos.delete - onBehalfOfContentOwner parameter

### Description
These methods now support the `onBehalfOfContentOwner` parameter, enabling authenticated YouTube CMS users to manage videos on behalf of a specified content owner.

### Method
POST (videos.insert), PUT (videos.update), DELETE (videos.delete)

### Endpoint
- /youtube/v3/videos (insert/update/delete)

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **onBehalfOfContentOwner** (string) - Optional - Specifies the content owner to act on behalf of. The authenticated user's CMS account must be linked to this content owner.
- **onBehalfOfContentOwnerChannel** (string) - Required when `onBehalfOfContentOwner` is used with `videos.insert`. Identifies the channel to which the video will be added. This channel must be linked to the specified content owner.
```

### YouTube Data API v3 - Code Sample Generation

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=tr

Illustrates the functionality of the APIs Explorer widget and the updated code samples tool for generating dynamic code samples. These samples are available for Java, JavaScript, PHP, Python, and curl, and dynamically update based on selected authorization scopes and parameter values.

```text
The APIs Explorer widget lets you select authorization scopes, enter sample parameter and property values, and then send actual API requests and see actual API responses. The widget also offers a fullscreen view that shows complete code samples, which dynamically update to use the scopes and values that you have entered.

Code samples are currently supported for Java, JavaScript, PHP, Python, and curl.
```

### March 11, 2015 Updates

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-tw

Details on updates released on March 11, 2015, including changes to the migration guide and feature support.

```APIDOC
## March 11, 2015 Updates

### Description
This section details changes introduced on March 11, 2015, focusing on the YouTube Data API v3 migration guide and feature support compared to the v2 API.

### Key Changes:

*   **YouTube Data API (v3) Migration Guide Updates:**
    *   A new tab 'New in the v3 API' has been added, listing features supported in v3 but not in v2.
    *   The v3 API will support the v2 API feature 'Flagging a video'.
    *   The following v2 API features will NOT be supported in v3:
        *   Retrieve video recommendations (use `activities.list` with `home=true` and check `snippet.type` for 'recommendation').
        *   Retrieve channel suggestions.
        *   Retrieve new subscription videos (use `activities.list` with `home=true` and check `snippet.type` for 'upload').
        *   RSS feed support.
        *   Push notifications for feed updates (v3 supports PubSubHubbub for video uploads and title/description updates only).

### Related Resources:

*   [YouTube Data API (v3) Migration Guide](/youtube/v3/migration-guide)
*   [Flagging a video (v2)](/youtube/2.0/developers_guide_protocol_complaints)
*   [Retrieve video recommendations (v2)](/youtube/2.0/developers_guide_protocol_recommendations)
*   [Retrieve channel suggestions (v2)](/youtube/2.0/developers_guide_protocol_channel_suggestions)
*   [Retrieve new subscription videos (v2)](/youtube/2.0/developers_guide_protocol_subscriptions#Retrieving_new_subscription_videos)
*   [API Query Parameters (v2) - alt=sp](/youtube/2.0/developers_guide_protocol_api_query_parameters#altsp)
*   [Sup (v2)](/youtube/2.0/developers_guide_protocol_sup)
*   [PubSubHubbub Protocol](https://github.com/pubsubhubbub/)

### API Methods Mentioned:

*   **`activities.list`**
    *   **Query Parameters:**
        *   `home` (boolean) - Optional - Set to `true` to retrieve activities for the authenticated user's home feed, which can include recommendations and uploads.
```

### YouTube API v3: Enhance search.list with forMine, order, and safeSearch parameters

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=vi

This update introduces new parameters to the search.list method for more refined searches. The 'forMine' parameter filters results to the authenticated user's videos, 'order' allows sorting by title or video count, and 'safeSearch' controls the inclusion of restricted content. No specific code examples are provided, but these parameters would be used in API requests.

```json
{
  "snippet": {
    "forMine": "true",
    "order": "title",
    "safeSearch": "strict"
  }
}
```

### Videos - List, Insert, Update with Live Streaming Details

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-tw

The videos.list, videos.insert, and videos.update methods now support the 'liveStreamingDetails' resource part. This allows retrieval of metadata related to live video broadcasts, including start and end times, and concurrent viewers.

```APIDOC
## GET/POST/PUT /youtube/v3/videos

### Description
Retrieves, inserts, or updates video resources. The `liveStreamingDetails` part can now be included in the `part` parameter to access live broadcast metadata.

### Method
GET, POST, PUT

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/videos

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - Comma-separated list of video resource parts to include in the API response. Include `liveStreamingDetails` to get live broadcast metadata.

#### Request Body (for POST/PUT)
- **snippet.liveBroadcastContent** (string) - The live broadcast content. Possible values: `active`, `none`.
- **liveStreamingDetails** (object) - Object containing metadata about a live video broadcast.
  - **actualStartTime** (datetime) - The time that the broadcast actually started. (Present when state is `active`.)
  - **actualEndTime** (datetime) - The time that the broadcast actually ended. (Present when broadcast is over.)
  - **scheduledStartTime** (datetime) - The time that the broadcast is scheduled to begin.
  - **scheduledEndTime** (datetime) - The time that the broadcast is scheduled to end. If empty or not present, the broadcast is scheduled indefinitely.
  - **concurrentViewers** (integer) - The number of people watching the live broadcast.

### Request Example (for videos.list with part)
```json
{
  "example": "GET /youtube/v3/videos?part=liveStreamingDetails&id=VIDEO_ID"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **items** (array) - List of video resources.
  - **liveStreamingDetails** (object) - Contains live broadcast metadata as described in the Request Body.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "example": "{\n  \"kind\": \"youtube#videoListResponse\",\n  \"etag\": \"...\",\n  \"items\": [\n    {\n      \"kind\": \"youtube#video\",\n      \"etag\": \"...\",\n      \"id\": \"VIDEO_ID\",\n      \"liveStreamingDetails\": {\n        \"actualStartTime\": \"2023-10-27T10:00:00Z\",\n        \"concurrentViewers\": 1500\n      }\n    }\n  ]\n}"
}
```
```

--------------------------------

### GET /playlistItems

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/docs/playlistItems

Returns a collection of playlist items that match the API request parameters. You can retrieve all of the playlist items in a specified playlist or retrieve one or more playlist items by their unique IDs.

```APIDOC
## GET /playlistItems

### Description
Returns a collection of playlist items that match the API request parameters. You can retrieve all of the playlist items in a specified playlist or retrieve one or more playlist items by their unique IDs.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/playlistItems`

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - The part of the playlist item resource that you want the API to return. Valid values are:
  - `snippet`
  - `contentDetails`
  - `status`
- **fields** (string) - Optional - A comma-separated list of fields to return. For example, `items(snippet/title,snippet/resourceId/videoId)`.
- **id** (string) - Optional - The ID of the playlist item.
- **maxResults** (unsigned integer) - Optional - The maximum number of results to return.
- **onBehalfOfContentOwner** (string) - Optional - Note: This parameter is intended for use by YouTube partners that own content and delegate management of that content to other representatives. As the onBehalfOfContentOwner parameter indicates that the request is being made on behalf of a content owner, the authenticated user must have the appropriate permissions to list content associated with that content owner. 
- **pageToken** (string) - Optional - The page token.
- **playlistId** (string) - Optional - The playlistId of the playlist for which to retrieve playlist items.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "example": "GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/playlistItems?part=snippet&playlistId=PL_z_8Ca23ue MjI0Y2Y4YjQ3YjA&key=YOUR_API_KEY"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **kind** (string) - Identifies this as a collection of playlist items.
- **etag** (string) - The ETag of the response.
- **nextPageToken** (string) - The token that can be used to retrieve the next page of results.
- **prevPageToken** (string) - The token that can be used to retrieve the previous page of results.
- **pageInfo** (object) - Information about the page of results.
  - **totalResults** (integer) - The total number of results.
  - **resultsPerPage** (integer) - The number of results per page.
- **items** (array) - A list of playlist items.
  - **kind** (string) - Identifies this as a playlist item.
  - **etag** (string) - The ETag of the response.
  - **id** (string) - The ID of the playlist item.
  - **snippet** (object) - The snippet of the playlist item.
    - **publishedAt** (datetime) - The date and time that the item was published.
    - **channelId** (string) - The ID of the channel that the item belongs to.
    - **title** (string) - The title of the playlist item.
    - **description** (string) - The description of the playlist item.
    - **thumbnails** (object) - The thumbnails for the playlist item.
    - **channelTitle** (string) - The title of the channel that the item belongs to.
    - **videoOwnerChannelTitle** (string) - The title of the channel that owns the video.
    - **videoOwnerChannelId** (string) - The ID of the channel that owns the video.
    - **playlistId** (string) - The ID of the playlist that the item belongs to.
    - **position** (unsigned integer) - The position of the item in the playlist.
    - **resourceId** (object) - The ID of the resource that is included in the playlist.
      - **kind** (string) - The kind of resource.
      - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the video.
  - **contentDetails** (object) - The content details of the playlist item.
    - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the video.
    - **startAt** (string) - The time in the video to begin playing.
    - **endAt** (string) - The time in the video to end playing.
    - **note** (string) - A note about the playlist item.
    - **videoPublishedAt** (datetime) - The date and time that the video was published.
  - **status** (object) - The status of the playlist item.
    - **privacyStatus** (string) - The privacy status of the playlist item.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "example": "{\n  \"kind\": \"youtube#playlistItemListResponse\",\n  \"etag\": \"_XhBJc6jnWe2EUEj6R10_4yX_4s\",\n  \"nextPageToken\": \"CDIQAA\",\n  \"pageInfo\": {\n    \"totalResults\": 100,\n    \"resultsPerPage\": 5\n  },\n  \"items\": [\n    {\n      \"kind\": \"youtube#playlistItem\",\n      \"etag\": \"_XhBJc6jnWe2EUEj6R10_4yX_4s\",\n      \"id\": \"UExfX3pfc2NBcjIz dWVNQ2k0Y2Y4YjQ3YjBfMC41QjY4RjQ2QjY0QzQ4QjQ3\",\n      \"snippet\": {\n        \"publishedAt\": \"2023-01-01T00:00:00Z\",\n        \"channelId\": \"UC-lHJZR3Gqxm24_Vd_AJsww\",\n        \"title\": \"Video Title 1\",\n        \"description\": \"Description for video 1.\",\n        \"thumbnails\": {\n          \"default\": {\n            \"url\": \"https://i.ytimg.com/vi/VIDEO_ID_1/default.jpg\",\n            \"width\": 120,\n            \"height\": 90\n          }\n        },\n        \"channelTitle\": \"Channel Title\",\n        \"videoOwnerChannelTitle\": \"Channel Title\",\n        \"videoOwnerChannelId\": \"UC-lHJZR3Gqxm24_Vd_AJsww\",\n        \"playlistId\": \"PL_z_8Ca23ueMjI0Y2Y4YjQ3YjA\",\n        \"position\": 0,\n        \"resourceId\": {\n          \"kind\": \"youtube#video\",\n          \"videoId\": \"VIDEO_ID_1\"\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  ]\n}"
}
```
```

### GET /youtube/v3/search - relatedToVideoId parameter update

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=vi

Clarification on the usage of the 'relatedToVideoId' parameter in the search.list method. When this parameter is set, only specific other parameters are supported.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/search

### Description
Updates to the `relatedToVideoId` parameter for the `search.list` method. If this parameter is set, the only other supported parameters are `part`, `maxResults`, `pageToken`, `regionCode`, `relevanceLanguage`, `safeSearch`, `type` (which must be set to `video`), and `fields`.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/search

### Query Parameters
- **relatedToVideoId** (string) - Specifies a video to which the search results should be related.
- **part** (string) - Identifies a list of YouTube Data API resources to include in the response.
- **maxResults** (integer) - The maximum number of results to return.
- **pageToken** (string) - The page token is used to request a specific page of results.
- **regionCode** (string) - Returns results of a YouTube video that are available in the specified region.
- **relevanceLanguage** (string) - Returns results that are relevant to the specified language.
- **safeSearch** (string) - Indicates whether the search results should be filtered for explicit content.
- **type** (string) - Specifies the type of results to return. Must be set to `video` when `relatedToVideoId` is used.
- **fields** (string) - Selector specifying which fields to include in a partial response.
```

```APIDOC
## API Compliance Audit and Quota Extension Process

### Description
All developers using YouTube's API Services must complete an API Compliance Audit to be granted more than the default quota allocation. New forms and guides are available to streamline this process.

### New Forms

*   **Audited Developer Requests Form:** For developers who have already passed an API Compliance Audit and need a quota extension.
    *   [https://support.google.com/youtube/contact/yt_api_audited_developer_requests_form](https://support.google.com/youtube/contact/yt_api_audited_developer_requests_form)
*   **Appeals Form:** For developers whose API projects have failed a compliance audit or been denied a quota increase.
    *   [https://support.google.com/youtube/contact/yt_api_appeals](https://support.google.com/youtube/contact/yt_api_appeals)
*   **Change of Control Form:** For developers experiencing a change of control associated with an API project.
    *   [https://support.google.com/youtube/contact/yt_api_change_of_control_form](https://support.google.com/youtube/contact/yt_api_change_of_control_form)

### Guide

    *   [/youtube/v3/guides/quota_and_compliance_audits](/youtube/v3/guides/quota_and_compliance_audits)

### GET /youtube/v3/search (Location Search)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=tr

The search.list method now supports the location and locationRadius parameters, enabling searches for videos associated with a specific geographic location.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/search

### Description
Searches for videos based on a specified geographic location. Both `location` and `locationRadius` parameters must be provided for location-based searches.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/search

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **location** (string) - Required - Latitude/longitude coordinates (e.g., "37.422, -122.084") at the center of the geographic area.
- **locationRadius** (string) - Required - Radius (in meters) around the `location` to search within (e.g., "10000m").

### Request Example
```json
GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/search?part=snippet&location=37.422,-122.084&locationRadius=10000m&key=YOUR_API_KEY
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **items** (array) - A list of search results, where each item contains video details.
  - **snippet.title** (string) - The title of the video.
  - **snippet.channelTitle** (string) - The title of the channel.
  - **snippet.publishedAt** (string) - The date and time the video was published.

#### Response Example
{
  "kind": "youtube#searchListResponse",
  "etag": "...",
  "nextPageToken": "...",
  "regionCode": "US",
  "pageInfo": {
    "totalResults": 100,
    "resultsPerPage": 10
  },
  "items": [
    {
      "kind": "youtube#searchResult",
      "etag": "...",
      "id": {
        "kind": "youtube#video",
        "videoId": "dQw4w9WgXcQ"
      },
      "snippet": {
        "publishedAt": "2011-03-01T00:10:00Z",
        "channelId": "UC_x5XG1OV2P6uZZ5FSM9Ttw",
        "title": "Rick Astley - Never Gonna Give You Up (Official Music Video)",
        "description": "
        ",
        "thumbnails": {
          "default": {
            "url": "https://i.ytimg.com/vi/dQw4w9WgXcQ/default.jpg"
          },
          "medium": {
            "url": "https://i.ytimg.com/vi/dQw4w9WgXcQ/mqdefault.jpg"
          },
          "high": {
            "url": "https://i.ytimg.com/vi/dQw4w9WgXcQ/hqdefault.jpg"
          }
        },
        "channelTitle": "Rick Astley",
        "liveBroadcastContent": "none",
        "publishTime": "2011-03-01T00:10:00Z"
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

### Description
Instructions for claiming live broadcast content, a prerequisite for showing ads during a broadcast. This process is specific to live videos and requires participation in the YouTube Content ID program.

### playlistItems.insert - invalid contentDetails

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=vi

The `playlistItems.insert` method returns an `invalidValue` error when the `contentDetails` object in the request is invalid, for example, if the `contentDetails.note` field exceeds 280 characters.

```APIDOC
## POST /youtube/v3/playlistItems

### Description
Inserts a new item into a playlist. This endpoint can return an `invalidValue` error if the provided `contentDetails` are malformed, such as an overly long `note`.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/playlistItems

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **contentDetails** (object) - Required - Contains details about the playlist item.
  - **note** (string) - Optional - A note to associate with the playlist item. Maximum length is 280 characters.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "example": {
    "contentDetails": {
      "note": "A very long note that exceeds the 280 character limit which will cause an invalidValue error."
    }
  }
}
```

### Response
#### Error Response (400)
- **error.code** (integer) - The HTTP status code, typically 400 for this error.
- **error.message** (string) - A descriptive error message.
- **error.errors[].reason** (string) - The specific reason for the error, e.g., `invalidContentDetails`.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "error": {
    "code": 400,
    "message": "Invalid content details.",
    "errors": [
      {
        "reason": "invalidContentDetails"
      }
    ]
  }
}
```
```

--------------------------------

### List Playlist Items - Go

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=th

Provides a Go code sample for listing playlist items using the YouTube Data API v3. This snippet demonstrates how to authenticate and fetch playlist items, potentially with content owner authorization.

```Go
package main

import (
	"context"
	"fmt"
	"log"

	"google.golang.org/api/option"
	"google.golang.org/api/youtube/v3"
)

func main() {
	ctx := context.Background()

	service, err := youtube.NewService(ctx, option.WithAPIKey("YOUR_API_KEY"))
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Unable to create YouTube service: %v", err)
	}

	playlistID := "YOUR_PLAYLIST_ID"

	call := service.PlaylistItems.List([]string{"snippet", "contentDetails"})
	call.PlaylistId(playlistID)
	call.MaxResults(50)

	// If operating on behalf of a content owner, uncomment the following lines:
	// call.OnBehalfOfContentOwner("YOUR_CONTENT_OWNER_ID")

	response, err := call.Do()
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Error fetching playlist items: %v", err)
	}

	fmt.Printf("Found %d playlist items:\n", len(response.Items))
	for _, item := range response.Items {
		fmt.Printf("%s\n", item.Snippet.Title)
	}
}

```

--------------------------------

### Subscriptions List - New Parameters

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-tw

Explains the addition of `onBehalfOfContentOwner` and `onBehalfOfContentOwnerChannel` parameters to the `subscriptions.list` method in the YouTube Data API v3.

```APIDOC
## Subscriptions List - New Parameters

### Description
This documentation covers the addition of new parameters to the `subscriptions.list` method, enabling content owner specific listing.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/subscriptions`

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
N/A

#### Query Parameters
*   **onBehalfOfContentOwner** (string) - Optional - Returns the subscriptions of the content owner specified in the parameter.
*   **onBehalfOfContentOwnerChannel** (string) - Optional - Returns the subscriptions of the content owner's channel specified in the parameter.

#### Request Body
N/A

### Request Example
`GET /youtube/v3/subscriptions?part=subscriberSnippet&onBehalfOfContentOwner=YOUR_CONTENT_OWNER_ID`

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **kind** (string) - Identifies this as a collection of subscription resources.
- **etag** (string) - The ETag of the response resource.
- **nextPageToken** (string) - The token that can be used to retrieve the next page of results.
- **prevPageToken** (string) - The token that can be used to retrieve the previous page of results.
- **pageInfo** (object) - Paging details for the results.
- **items** (array) - A list of subscription resources.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "kind": "youtube#subscriptionListResponse",
  "etag": "YOUR_ETAG",
  "pageInfo": {
    "totalResults": 100,
    "resultsPerPage": 5
  },
  "items": [
    {
      "kind": "youtube#subscription",
      "etag": "ITEM_ETAG",
      "id": "YOUR_SUBSCRIPTION_ID",
      "snippet": {
        "publishedAt": "2023-01-01T00:00:00Z",
        "channelId": "TARGET_CHANNEL_ID",
        "title": "Subscribed Channel Title",
        "description": "Subscribed channel description.",
        "resourceId": {
          "kind": "youtube#channel",
          "channelId": "TARGET_CHANNEL_ID"
        }
      }
    }
  ]
}
```
```

### Handle Account Delegation Forbidden Error (YouTube API v3)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=tr

This example shows how to handle the 'forbidden' error with the 'accountDelegationForbidden' reason code when using the YouTube Data API v3. This error typically occurs when account delegation is not permitted.

```javascript
gapi.client.youtube.videos.getRating({
  "id": "VIDEO_ID"
}).then(function(response) {
  // Process successful response
}, function(err) {
  if (err.result.error.code === 403 && err.result.error.message === 'Forbidden' && err.result.error.errors[0].reason === 'accountDelegationForbidden') {
    console.error('Account delegation is forbidden for this action.');
  } else {
    console.error('An error occurred:', err);
  }
});
```

### YouTube API: Insert Activity (Go)

```Go
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"log"

	"google.golang.org/api/youtube/v3"
)

func main() {
	// Assume client is an authorized *http.Client
	sservice, err := youtube.New(client)
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Error creating YouTube client: %v", err)
	}

	call := service.Activities.Insert("snippet", &youtube.Activity{})
	// Set parameters as needed, e.g., part, onBehalfOfContentOwner

	response, err := call.Do()
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Error making API call to insert activity: %v", err)
	}

	fmt.Printf("Activity inserted: %+v\n", response)
}

### Search YouTube Content by Keyword in C#

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/code_samples/dotnet

This C# code snippet demonstrates how to use the YouTube Data API v3's `search.list` method to find videos, channels, and playlists associated with a given keyword. It requires the Google APIs Client Library for .NET and an API key. The output categorizes the search results into videos, channels, and playlists.

```csharp
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.IO;
using System.Reflection;
using System.Threading;
using System.Threading.Tasks;

using Google.Apis.Auth.OAuth2;
using Google.Apis.Services;
using Google.Apis.Upload;
using Google.Apis.Util.Store;
using Google.Apis.YouTube.v3;
using Google.Apis.YouTube.v3.Data;

namespace Google.Apis.YouTube.Samples
{
  /// <summary>
  /// YouTube Data API v3 sample: search by keyword.
  /// Relies on the Google APIs Client Library for .NET, v1.7.0 or higher.
  /// See https://developers.google.com/api-client-library/dotnet/get_started
  ///
  /// Set ApiKey to the API key value from the APIs & auth > Registered apps tab of
  ///   https://cloud.google.com/console
  /// Please ensure that you have enabled the YouTube Data API for your project.
  /// </summary>
  internal class Search
  {
    [STAThread]
    static void Main(string[] args)
    {
      Console.WriteLine("YouTube Data API: Search");
      Console.WriteLine("========================");

      try
      {
        new Search().Run().Wait();
      }
      catch (AggregateException ex)
      {
        foreach (var e in ex.InnerExceptions)
        {
          Console.WriteLine("Error: " + e.Message);
        }
      }

      Console.WriteLine("Press any key to continue...");
      Console.ReadKey();
    }

    private async Task Run()
    {
      var youtubeService = new YouTubeService(new BaseClientService.Initializer()
      {
        ApiKey = "REPLACE_ME",
        ApplicationName = this.GetType().ToString()
      });

      var searchListRequest = youtubeService.Search.List("snippet");
      searchListRequest.Q = "Google"; // Replace with your search term.
      searchListRequest.MaxResults = 50;

      // Call the search.list method to retrieve results matching the specified query term.
      var searchListResponse = await searchListRequest.ExecuteAsync();

      List<string> videos = new List<string>();
      List<string> channels = new List<string>();
      List<string> playlists = new List<string>();

      // Add each result to the appropriate list, and then display the lists of
      // matching videos, channels, and playlists.
      foreach (var searchResult in searchListResponse.Items)
      {
        switch (searchResult.Id.Kind)
        {
          case "youtube#video":
            videos.Add(String.Format("{0} ({1})", searchResult.Snippet.Title, searchResult.Id.VideoId));
            break;

          case "youtube#channel":
            channels.Add(String.Format("{0} ({1})", searchResult.Snippet.Title, searchResult.Id.ChannelId));
            break;

          case "youtube#playlist":
            playlists.Add(String.Format("{0} ({1})", searchResult.Snippet.Title, searchResult.Id.PlaylistId));
            break;
        }
      }

      Console.WriteLine(String.Format("Videos:\n{0}\n", string.Join("\n", videos)));
      Console.WriteLine(String.Format("Channels:\n{0}\n", string.Join("\n", channels)));
      Console.WriteLine(String.Format("Playlists:\n{0}\n", string.Join("\n", playlists)));
    }
  }
}

```

### guideCategories.list - Error Handling

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=tr

Information on the 'notFound' error type for the guideCategories.list method in the YouTube Data API v3.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/guideCategories

### Description
Retrieves a list of YouTube guide categories.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/guideCategories

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **id** (string) - Required - The ID of the guide category to retrieve.

### Response
#### Error Response
- **code** (integer) - The error code (e.g., 404).
- **message** (string) - A description of the error. For this method, it could be 'notFound'.
- **errors** (array)
  - **reason** (string) - The specific reason for the error, e.g., 'videoCategoryNotFound'.
  - **message** (string) - A human-readable explanation of the error.
  - **domain** (string) - The domain of the error.

#### Error Example (404)
```json
{
  "code": 404,
  "message": "Not Found",
  "errors": [
    {
      "reason": "notFound",
      "message": "The guide category identified by the id parameter cannot be found."
    }
  ]
}
```

### GET /youtube/v3/search - order parameter update

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=vi

Updates to the 'order' parameter for the search.list method. Sorting live broadcasts by 'viewCount' will now sort by concurrent viewers during the broadcast.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/search

### Description
Updates to the `order` parameter for the `search.list` method. If you sort live broadcasts by `viewCount`, the API results are sorted by the broadcasts' number of concurrent viewers while the broadcasts are still ongoing.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/search

### Query Parameters
- **order** (string) - Specifies the order of results. If set to `viewCount` for live broadcasts, results are sorted by concurrent viewers.
```

### Upload Video using YouTube Data API v3 in Go

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/code_samples/go

This Go program uploads a video file to YouTube using the `videos.insert` method of the YouTube Data API v3. It requires authentication via OAuth 2.0 and accepts command-line flags for specifying the video file, title, description, category, keywords, and privacy status. The code handles file operations and API interactions, outputting the uploaded video's ID upon success.

```Go
package main

import (
	"flag"
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"os"
	"strings"

	"google.golang.org/api/youtube/v3"
)

var (
	filename    = flag.String("filename", "", "Name of video file to upload")
	title       = flag.String("title", "Test Title", "Video title")
description = flag.String("description", "Test Description", "Video description")
	category    = flag.String("category", "22", "Video category")
	keywords    = flag.String("keywords", "", "Comma separated list of video keywords")
	privacy     = flag.String("privacy", "unlisted", "Video privacy status")
)

func main() {
	flag.Parse()

	if *filename == "" {
		log.Fatalf("You must provide a filename of a video file to upload")
	}

	client := getClient(youtube.YoutubeUploadScope)

	service, err := youtube.New(client)
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Error creating YouTube client: %v", err)
	}

	upload := &youtube.Video{
		Snippet: &youtube.VideoSnippet{
			Title:       *title,
			Description: *description,
			CategoryId:  *category,
		},
		Status: &youtube.VideoStatus{PrivacyStatus: *privacy},
	}

	// The API returns a 400 Bad Request response if tags is an empty string.
	if strings.Trim(*keywords, "") != "" {
		upload.Snippet.Tags = strings.Split(*keywords, ",")
	}

	call := service.Videos.Insert("snippet,status", upload)

	file, err := os.Open(*filename)
	defer file.Close()
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Error opening %v: %v", *filename, err)
	}

	response, err := call.Media(file).Do()
	handleError(err, "")
	fmt.Printf("Upload successful! Video ID: %v\n", response.Id)
}

```

### Generate Token Cache File Path (Go)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/code_samples/go

Generates a file path for storing OAuth2 token credentials. It constructs a path within the user's home directory under a '.credentials' folder, ensuring the directory exists. The filename is derived from the URL, properly escaped. This function helps in managing persistent token storage.

```go
// tokenCacheFile generates credential file path/filename.
// It returns the generated credential path/filename.
func tokenCacheFile() (string, error) {
	usr, err := user.Current()
	if err != nil {
		return "", err
	}
	tokenCacheDir := filepath.Join(usr.HomeDir, ".credentials")
	os.MkdirAll(tokenCacheDir, 0700)
	return filepath.Join(tokenCacheDir,
		url.QueryEscape("youtube-go.json")), err
}
```

### Get YouTube Video Embed HTML with Dynamic Sizing (YouTube API v3)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=tr

```json

    "part": "player",
    "id": "VIDEO_ID",
    "maxHeight": 720,
    "maxWidth": 1280
  }
}

### Retrieving All Localizations

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=vi

To get all available localized details for a resource, include `localizations` in the `part` parameter. This is useful for checking availability in languages not directly supported by the `hl` parameter.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/{resourceType}

### Description
When retrieving resources, including `localizations` in the `part` parameter allows you to fetch all available localized details. This enables you to programmatically check for the existence of localized text in specific languages, even if they are not standard YouTube application languages.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/channels
/youtube/v3/channelSections
/youtube/v3/playlists
/youtube/v3/videos

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - Specifies the parts of the resource to be included. Include `localizations` to retrieve all available localized data.

### Request Example
```http
GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/videos.list?part=snippet,localizations&id=VIDEO_ID
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **snippet.localizations** (object) - An object containing key-value pairs where keys are language codes and values are objects with localized `title` and `description`.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "kind": "youtube#video",
  "etag": "...",
  "items": [
    {
      "kind": "youtube#video",
      "etag": "...",
      "id": "VIDEO_ID",
      "snippet": {
        "title": "Playing soccer",
        "description": "We play soccer in the park on Sundays.",
        "defaultLanguage": "en",
        "localizations": {
          "de": {
            "title": "Fuball spielen",
            "description": "Wir spielen Fuball im Park am Sonntag"
          },
          "fr": {
            "title": "Jouer au football",
            "description": "Nous jouons au football dans le parc le dimanche"
          }
        }
      }
    }
  ]
}
```
```

### YouTube Data API v3 - Partial Resources (`part` and `fields` parameters)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/getting-started

This section details how to use the `part` and `fields` parameters to retrieve only the necessary data from API responses, optimizing performance and reducing data transfer.

```APIDOC
## Partial Resources

### Description
The `part` and `fields` parameters are essential for optimizing API requests by allowing you to specify exactly which data you want to retrieve, thereby reducing bandwidth usage and improving response times.

### The `part` Parameter
*   **Purpose**: The `part` parameter is mandatory for most resource retrieval requests. It specifies which resource properties (or 'parts') should be included in the response.
*   **Usage**: You provide a comma-separated list of part names. For example, to retrieve a video's title, description, and thumbnail, you might use `part=snippet`.
*   **Example**: `GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/videos?id=VIDEO_ID&part=snippet,statistics`

### The `fields` Parameter
*   **Purpose**: The `fields` parameter provides a more granular way to filter the response, allowing you to select specific nested properties within the parts you've requested.
*   **Usage**: It uses a syntax similar to XPath to navigate the JSON response structure. You can select specific fields, arrays, or slices of arrays.
*   **Example**: `GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/videos?id=VIDEO_ID&part=snippet&fields=items(snippet(title,description))`
    *   This request retrieves only the `title` and `description` from the `snippet` part of the video resource.

### Sample Partial Requests
*   **Requesting only video title and channel ID**:
    ```
    GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/videos?id=dQw4w9WgXcQ&part=snippet&fields=items(snippet(title,channelId))
    ```
*   **Requesting video statistics (view count, like count)**:
    ```
    GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/videos?id=dQw4w9WgXcQ&part=statistics&fields=items(statistics(viewCount,likeCount))
    ```

### Benefits
*   **Reduced Data Transfer**: Significantly decreases the amount of data transferred over the network.
*   **Improved Performance**: Faster response times due to smaller payloads.
*   **Lower Quota Consumption**: Can help reduce quota usage by avoiding the retrieval of unnecessary data.
```

--------------------------------

### Captions API - OnBehalfOfContentOwner Parameter

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=vi

The captions.delete, captions.download, captions.insert, captions.list, and captions.update methods now support the onBehalfOfContentOwner parameter. Requests using this parameter require authorization with the youtubepartner scope.
