## POST /youtube/v3/captions

### Description
This endpoint is part of the captions resource and supports operations like delete, download, insert, list, and update. It now includes the `onBehalfOfContentOwner` parameter.

### Method
POST (for insert/update), GET (for list/download), DELETE (for delete)

### Endpoint
`/youtube/v3/captions

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **onBehalfOfContentOwner** (string) - Optional - Identifies the content owner to be used when authorized via a third-party token. This parameter is required for requests made on behalf of a content owner.

### Request Body
(Varies based on the specific caption operation: insert, update)

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
(Varies based on the specific caption operation)

#### Error Response
(Standard YouTube API errors apply)

### Authorization
Requests using `onBehalfOfContentOwner` require a token with the `https://www.googleapis.com/auth/youtubepartner` scope.
```

### thumbnails.set Code Samples

## POST /youtube/v3/thumbnails/set

### Description
Sets a custom thumbnail image for a video. Code samples are available.

POST

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/thumbnails/set

### Parameters

- **videoId** (string) - Required - The ID of the video for which the thumbnail is set.

#### Request Body
- **title** (string) - Required - The title of the thumbnail.
- **data** (string) - Required - Base64 encoded image data.
- **mimeType** (string) - Required - The MIME type of the image (e.g., "image/png").

  "title": "My Custom Thumbnail",
  "data": "BASE64_ENCODED_IMAGE_DATA",
  "mimeType": "image/jpeg"
}

### GET /youtube/v3/search - RelatedToVideoId Parameter Update

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-cn

The 'relatedToVideoId' parameter for the search.list method has been updated with a list of mutually supported parameters. This update clarifies usage but does not change API behavior.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/search

### Description
Updates to the `search.list` method's `relatedToVideoId` parameter note that when this parameter is set, only specific other parameters are supported. This clarification does not alter the API's behavior.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/search

### Query Parameters
- **relatedToVideoId** (string) - Optional - Specifies a video to which the search results should be related.
- **part** (string) - Optional - Specifies the parts of the search results to include.
- **maxResults** (integer) - Optional - The maximum number of results to return.
- **pageToken** (string) - Optional - The page token to retrieve the next page of results.
- **regionCode** (string) - Optional - Returns results relevant to a particular region.
- **relevanceLanguage** (string) - Optional - Returns results relevant to a particular language.
- **safeSearch** (string) - Optional - Indicates whether to exclude certain results from search results.
- **type** (string) - Optional - If set, must be `video`. Specifies the type of search results to return.
- **fields** (string) - Optional - A comma-separated list of fields to return.
```

### playlistItems.list and playlistItems.insert

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-cn

These methods now support the onBehalfOfContentOwner parameter for operations related to playlist items.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/playlistItems
## POST /youtube/v3/playlistItems

### Description
Retrieves or inserts playlist items. Supports the `onBehalfOfContentOwner` parameter for actions performed on behalf of a content owner.

### Method
GET (for list), POST (for insert)

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/playlistItems

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **onBehalfOfContentOwner** (string) - Optional - The onBehalfOfContentOwner parameter identifies the content owner that the user is acting on behalf of.

#### Request Body (for playlistItems.insert)
- **snippet.playlistId** (string) - Required - The playlist ID to insert the item into.
- **snippet.resourceId.kind** (string) - Required - The kind of resource, e.g. "youtube#video".
- **snippet.resourceId.videoId** (string) - Required - The ID of the video to insert.
```

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/getting-started_hl=id

This example demonstrates using the 'fields' parameter to remove 'kind' and 'etag' properties from the API response. It also implicitly excludes 'contentDetails' and 'status' by not specifying them in the 'fields' parameter.

```json
{
 "videos": [
  {
   "id": "7lCDEYXw3mM",
   "snippet": {
    "publishedAt": "2012-06-20T22:45:24.000Z",
    "channelId": "UC_x5XG1OV2P6uZZ5FSM9Ttw",
    "title": "Google I/O 101: Q&A On Using Google APIs",
    "description": "Antonio Fuentes speaks to us and takes questions on working with Google APIs and OAuth 2.0.",
    "thumbnails": {
     "default": {
      "url": "https://i.ytimg.com/vi/7lCDEYXw3mM/default.jpg"
     },
     "medium": {
      "url": "https://i.ytimg.com/vi/7lCDEYXw3mM/mqdefault.jpg"
     },
     "high": {
      "url": "https://i.ytimg.com/vi/7lCDEYXw3mM/hqdefault.jpg"
     }
    },
    "categoryId": "28"
   },
   "statistics": {
    "viewCount": "3057",
    "likeCount": "25",
    "dislikeCount": "0",
    "favoriteCount": "17",
    "commentCount": "12"

 ]
}

### YouTube API v3: Handle channelNotFound error for channels.update

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-tw

This code example illustrates how to handle the 'channelNotFound' error when using the 'channels.update' method in the YouTube Data API v3. This error is returned if the specified channel ID does not exist. Developers should ensure the provided channel ID is correct before making the API call.

```json
{
  "error": {
    "code": 404,
    "message": "Not Found.",
    "errors": [
      {
        "domain": "global",
        "reason": "channelNotFound",
        "message": "Not Found."
      }
    ],
    "status": "NOT_FOUND"
  }
}
```

### Captions API - onBehalfOfContentOwner Parameter

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=tr

The captions.delete, captions.download, captions.insert, captions.list, and captions.update methods now support the onBehalfOfContentOwner parameter. Requests using this parameter require authorization with the youtubepartner scope.

```APIDOC
## Captions API Updates

### Description
Several methods within the Captions API have been updated to include the `onBehalfOfContentOwner` parameter. This allows for operations to be performed on behalf of a content owner.

### Methods
- `captions.delete`
- `captions.download`
- `captions.insert`
- `captions.list`
- `captions.update`

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **onBehalfOfContentOwner** (string) - Optional - The ID of the content owner when acting on behalf of a content owner.

### Authorization
Requests using the `onBehalfOfContentOwner` parameter require the `https://www.googleapis.com/auth/youtubepartner` scope.
```

--------------------------------

### Captions API - onBehalfOfContentOwner Parameter

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-tw

The captions.delete, captions.download, captions.insert, captions.list, and captions.update methods now support the onBehalfOfContentOwner parameter. Requests using this parameter require the youtube.partner scope.

```APIDOC
## Update: captions API methods

### Description
The following captions API methods now support the `onBehalfOfContentOwner` parameter:
- `captions.delete`
- `captions.download`
- `captions.insert`
- `captions.list`
- `captions.update`

### Authorization
Requests using the `onBehalfOfContentOwner` parameter require a token with the `https://www.googleapis.com/auth/youtubepartner` scope.

### Invideo Promotion Requirements

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/docs/channels/update

This section details the required fields and their descriptions for setting up an invideo promotion. It covers timing types, timing details, video IDs, and website URLs.

```APIDOC
## Invideo Promotion Requirements

### Description
This section details the required fields and their descriptions for setting up an invideo promotion. It covers timing types, timing details, video IDs, and website URLs.

### Method
POST (Implied, as these are request body requirements)

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/invideoPromotions (Implied)

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **invideoPromotion.defaultTiming.type** (string) - Required - The request metadata must specify a timing method so that YouTube can determine when to display the promoted item.
- **invideoPromotion.timing.type** (string) - Required - The request metadata must specify a timing method so that YouTube can determine when to display the promoted item.
- **invideoPromotion** (object) - Required - The request metadata must specify a timing for each item in the `invideoPromotion` part.
- **invideoPromotion.items[].id.videoId** (string) - Required - The request metadata must specify a video ID to identify the promoted item.
- **invideoPromotion.items[].id.websiteUrl** (string) - Required - The request metadata must specify a website URL in the invideoPromotion part.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "invideoPromotion": {
    "defaultTiming": {
      "type": "later"
    },
    "timing": {
      "type": "later"
    },
    "items": [
      {
        "id": {
          "videoId": "VIDEO_ID_HERE",
          "websiteUrl": "WEBSITE_URL_HERE"
        }
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

### Response
#### Error Response (400 Bad Request)
- **code** (integer) - The error code.
- **message** (string) - A description of the error.
- **errors** (array) - An array of detailed error objects.
  - **reason** (string) - The reason for the error (e.g., "requiredTimingType", "requiredVideoId").
  - **message** (string) - A description of the specific error.
  - **domain** (string) - The domain of the error.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "error": {
    "code": 400,
    "message": "Required properties missing from the request.",
    "errors": [
      {
        "reason": "requiredTimingType",
        "message": "The request metadata must specify a timing method so that YouTube can determine when to display the promoted item. Set the value of the `invideoPromotion.defaultTiming.type` property in the resource that the request sends.",
        "domain": "global"
      }
    ]
  }
}
```
```

### YouTube API v3: Video Rate Method Parameter Correction

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=th

Corrects the documentation for the videos.rate method, clarifying that the onBehalfOfContentOwner parameter is not supported. Attempting to use this parameter results in a 500 error.

```text
The parameter list for the videos.rate method has been updated to reflect that that method does not actually support the onBehalfOfContentOwner parameter. This was a documentation error as videos.rate requests that set this parameter return a 500 error.
```

### Search by Keyword

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/code_samples/go

Searches for videos, channels, and playlists on YouTube based on provided keywords. Utilizes command-line flags for specifying search terms and other parameters.

```APIDOC
## Search by Keyword

### Description
This endpoint allows you to search YouTube for videos, channels, and playlists using keywords. You can specify various search parameters via command-line flags to refine your search results.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/search`

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
None

#### Query Parameters
- **q** (string) - Required - The search query (keywords).
- **type** (string) - Optional - The type of resource to search for (e.g., `video`, `channel`, `playlist`).
- **maxResults** (integer) - Optional - The maximum number of results to return.
- **pageToken** (string) - Optional - The page token for the next page of results.

#### Request Body
None

### Request Example
```bash
go run main.go --q="golang tutorial" --type=video --maxResults=10
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **items** (array) - A list of search result resources.
  - **id** (object) - The ID of the resource.
    - **kind** (string) - The type of resource (e.g., `youtube#video`).
    - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the video.
    - **channelId** (string) - The ID of the channel.
    - **playlistId** (string) - The ID of the playlist.
  - **snippet** (object) - The snippet of the resource.
    - **title** (string) - The title of the resource.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "items": [
    {
      "id": {
        "kind": "youtube#video",
        "videoId": "VIDEO_ID_1"
      },
      "snippet": {
        "title": "Go Programming Language Tutorial"
      }
    }
  ]
}
```
```

### Video Insertion, Update, and Deletion - New onBehalfOfContentOwner Parameter

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=vi

The onBehalfOfContentOwner parameter is now supported for videos.insert, videos.update, and videos.delete, enabling content owners to manage videos across their channels.

```APIDOC
## Videos API - onBehalfOfContentOwner Parameter

### Description
The `onBehalfOfContentOwner` parameter allows authorized YouTube CMS users to perform operations (insert, update, delete) on videos across channels associated with a specified content owner. When used with `videos.insert`, `onBehalfOfContentOwnerChannel` must also be specified.

### Method
POST (videos.insert), PUT (videos.update), DELETE (videos.delete)

### Endpoint
- `/youtube/v3/videos/insert`
- `/youtube/v3/videos/update`
- `/youtube/v3/videos/delete`

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **onBehalfOfContentOwner** (string) - Required for content owner operations - Identifies the content owner on whose behalf the request is being made.
- **onBehalfOfContentOwnerChannel** (string) - Required for `videos.insert` when `onBehalfOfContentOwner` is used - Identifies the channel to which the video will be added.

### Request Example (videos.insert)
```json
{
  "example": "POST /youtube/v3/videos/insert?onBehalfOfContentOwner=CHANNEL_OWNER_ID&onBehalfOfContentOwnerChannel=TARGET_CHANNEL_ID\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  \"kind\": \"youtube#video\",\n  \"snippet\": {\n    \"title\": \"My New Video\",\n    \"description\": \"This is a great video!\",\n    \"tags\": [\"tutorial\", \"youtube\"]\n  },\n  \"status\": {\n    \"privacyStatus\": \"public\"\n  }\n}"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **id** (string) - The unique identifier for the video.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "example": "{\n  \"kind\": \"youtube#video\",\n  \"etag\": \"...\",\n  \"id\": \"VIDEO_ID\",\n  \"snippet\": {\n    \"publishedAt\": \"2023-10-27T10:00:00Z\",\n    \"channelId\": \"TARGET_CHANNEL_ID\",\n    \"title\": \"My New Video\",\n    \"description\": \"This is a great video!\",\n    \"tags\": [\"tutorial\", \"youtube\"]\n  },\n  \"status\": {\n    \"privacyStatus\": \"public\"\n  }\n}"
}
```
```

### Retrieve User's Uploaded Videos (C#)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/docs/playlistItems/list

This C# code snippet retrieves the playlist ID for a user's uploaded videos using the `channels.list` method and then iterates through the playlist items using `playlistItems.list` to display each video's title and ID. It handles pagination to fetch all uploaded videos.

```csharp
var channelsListResponse = await channelsListRequest.ExecuteAsync();

      foreach (var channel in channelsListResponse.Items)
      {
        // From the API response, extract the playlist ID that identifies the list
        // of videos uploaded to the authenticated user's channel.
        var uploadsListId = channel.ContentDetails.RelatedPlaylists.Uploads;

        Console.WriteLine("Videos in list {0}", uploadsListId);

        var nextPageToken = "";
        while (nextPageToken != null)
        {
          var playlistItemsListRequest = youtubeService.PlaylistItems.List("snippet");
          playlistItemsListRequest.PlaylistId = uploadsListId;
          playlistItemsListRequest.MaxResults = 50;
          playlistItemsListRequest.PageToken = nextPageToken;

          // Retrieve the list of videos uploaded to the authenticated user's channel.
          var playlistItemsListResponse = await playlistItemsListRequest.ExecuteAsync();

          foreach (var playlistItem in playlistItemsListResponse.Items)
          {
            // Print information about each video.
            Console.WriteLine("{0} ({1})", playlistItem.Snippet.Title, playlistItem.Snippet.ResourceId.VideoId);
          }

          nextPageToken = playlistItemsListResponse.NextPageToken;
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
```

## POST /youtube/v3/videos

### Description

#### Request Body
- **snippet.title** (string) - Required - The title of the video.
- **snippet.description** (string) - Optional - The description of the video.
- **snippet.tags** (array of strings) - Optional - Tags associated with the video.
- **snippet.categoryId** (string) - Optional - The category ID for the video.

    "description": "This is a description of my awesome video.",
    "tags": ["tag1", "tag2"],
    "categoryId": "22"
  },
  "status": {
    "privacyStatus": "public"

### GET /youtube/v3/search - Location Parameters

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-cn

The search.list method now supports 'location' and 'locationRadius' parameters, enabling geographically targeted video searches. Both parameters must be provided to use location-based filtering.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/search

### Description
This endpoint allows you to search YouTube for videos. New parameters 'location' and 'locationRadius' have been added to enable searching for videos within a specified geographic area. Both parameters are required for location-based searches.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/search

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - Specifies the search resource parts you want to retrieve. Example: `snippet`
- **q** (string) - Optional - The query term that will cause YouTube to return matching video resources.
- **location** (string) - Required (if locationRadius is used) - Specifies the latitude/longitude coordinates at the center of the geographic area. Format: `latitude,longitude`. Example: `37.422,-122.084`
- **locationRadius** (string) - Required (if location is used) - Specifies the radius around the location in kilometers or miles. Example: `10km` or `5mi`.

### Request Example
```bash
GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/search?part=snippet&q=Gamer+Setup&location=37.422,-122.084&locationRadius=5km
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **items** (array) - A list of search results.
  - **kind** (string) - The type of the API resource.
  - **etag** (string) - The ETag of the resource.
  - **id** (object) - The id object contains the ID of the resource.
    - **kind** (string) - The kind of the resource (e.g., `youtube#video`).
    - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the video.
  - **snippet** (object) - Contains details about the search result.
    - **publishedAt** (string) - The date and time that the video was published.
    - **channelId** (string) - The ID of the channel that published the video.
    - **title** (string) - The title of the video.
    - **description** (string) - The description of the video.
    - **thumbnails** (object) - A set of thumbnail images associated with the video.
    - **channelTitle** (string) - The title of the channel that published the video.
    - **liveBroadcastContent** (string) - Whether the video is a live broadcast.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "kind": "youtube#searchListResponse",
  "etag": "ETAG",
  "nextPageToken": "NEXT_PAGE_TOKEN",
  "regionCode": "US",
  "items": [
    {
      "kind": "youtube#searchResult",
      "etag": "ETAG",
      "id": {
        "kind": "youtube#video",
        "videoId": "VIDEO_ID"
      },
      "snippet": {
        "publishedAt": "2023-10-26T10:00:00Z",
        "channelId": "CHANNEL_ID",
        "title": "Example Video Title",
        "description": "This is a description of the example video.",
        "thumbnails": {
          "default": {"url": "URL"},
          "medium": {"url": "URL"},
          "high": {"url": "URL"}
        },
        "channelTitle": "Example Channel",
        "liveBroadcastContent": "none"
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

### Error Handling
- **400 Bad Request**: If only one of `location` or `locationRadius` is provided.
```

### Retrieving All Localizations

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-cn

To get all available localized details for a resource, include 'localizations' in the 'part' parameter. This is useful for checking if localized text exists for languages not currently supported as application languages.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/{resource}

### Description
Retrieves all localized details for a given resource by including 'localizations' in the 'part' parameter.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/youtube/v3/{resource}` (e.g., `/youtube/v3/videos`)

### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - Specifies the parts of the resource to retrieve. Include 'localizations' to get all available localized data.

### Request Example
```
GET /youtube/v3/videos?part=localizations&id=dQw4w9WgXcQ
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **localizations** (object) - An object containing all available localized details for the resource.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "kind": "youtube#videoListResponse",
  "etag": "...",
  "items": [
    {
      "kind": "youtube#video",
      "etag": "...",
      "id": "dQw4w9WgXcQ",
      "localizations": {
        "de": {
          "title": "Fuball spielen",
          "description": "Wir spielen Fuball im Park am Sonntag"
        },
        "fr": {
          "title": "Jouer au football",
          "description": "Nous jouons au football dans le parc le dimanche"
        }
      }
    }
  ]
}
```
```

### Configure PubSubHubbub for YouTube Data API v3 Push Notifications

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=vi

This outlines the configuration for using PubSubHubbub protocol for push notifications with the YouTube Data API v3. Unlike v2, v3 notifications are limited to video uploads and updates to video titles or descriptions. This is a conceptual example of how PubSubHubbub might be integrated.

```python
import pubsubhubbub.subscriber

SUBSCRIBERS = [
    'https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/subscriptions?part=snippet&mine=true&key=YOUR_API_KEY'
]

# Example of how a callback might handle a notification
def on_push_notification(topic, data):
    print(f'Received notification for topic: {topic}\nData: {data}')
    # Process the notification data (e.g., new video upload, title/description update)


if __name__ == '__main__':
    hub = pubsubhubbub.subscriber.HubSubscriber(SUBSCRIBERS, verify_token='YOUR_VERIFY_TOKEN')
    hub.listen(callback=on_push_notification)

```

--------------------------------

### List Search Results - Go

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=th

Provides a Go code sample for searching YouTube using the YouTube Data API v3. This snippet demonstrates how to authenticate and perform searches, including filtering by live broadcast content.

```Go
package main

import (
	"context"
	"fmt"
	"log"

	"google.golang.org/api/option"
	"google.golang.org/api/youtube/v3"
)

func main() {
	ctx := context.Background()

	service, err := youtube.NewService(ctx, option.WithAPIKey("YOUR_API_KEY"))
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Unable to create YouTube service: %v", err)
	}

	call := service.Search.List([]string{"snippet"})
	call.Q("go programming")
	call.Type("video")
	call.MaxResults(10)
	// To find live broadcast content, uncomment the following line:
	// call.LiveBroadcastContent("live") // or "upcoming", "none"

	response, err := call.Do()
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Error fetching search results: %v", err)
	}

	fmt.Printf("Found %d search results:\n", len(response.Items))
	for _, item := range response.Items {
		fmt.Printf("%s (%s)\n", item.Snippet.Title, item.Id.VideoId)
	}
}

```

```Python
import googleapiclient.discovery


def update_channel(youtube, channel_id, body):
    """Updates a channel's branding settings.

    Args:
        youtube: An authorized YouTube API service instance.
        channel_id: The ID of the channel to update.
        body: A dictionary representing the channel resource to update.
              Example: {'brandingSettings': {'channel': {'unsubscribedTrailer': 'VIDEO_ID'}}}
    """
    request = youtube.channels().update(
        part="brandingSettings",
        id=channel_id,
        body=body
    )
    response = request.execute()
    print(f"Channel {channel_id} updated successfully.")
    # The response contains the updated channel resource.

Rates a video. This method has been updated to reflect that the `onBehalfOfContentOwner` parameter is not supported and will result in a 500 error if used.

### Endpoint

- **id** (string) - Required - The id of the video to rate.

#### Request Body
This method does not support a request body.

### Request Example

  "id": "VIDEO_ID",
  "rating": "like"
}
```

No content is returned upon successful rate.

#### Response Example

### Search YouTube Videos, Channels, and Playlists by Keyword in Go

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/code_samples/go

This Go program searches the YouTube Data API for videos, channels, and playlists based on provided keywords. It uses command-line flags for search terms and other parameters. Requires OAuth 2.0 authorization.

```go
package main

import (
	"context"
	"flag"
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"net/http"

	"golang.org/x/oauth2"
	"google.golang.org/api/option"
	"google.golang.org/api/youtube/v3"
)

func search(client *http.Client) {
	ctx := context.Background()
	youtubeService, err := youtube.NewService(ctx, option.WithHTTPClient(client))
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Error creating YouTube client: %v", err)
	}

	var query string
	flag.StringVar(&query, "query", "", "Search query.")
	flag.Parse()

	if query == "" {
		log.Fatal("You must provide a search query using the -query flag.")
	}

	call := youtubeService.Search.List([]string{"snippet"})
	call.Q(query)
	call.Type("video,channel,playlist") // Search for videos, channels, and playlists
	call.MaxResults(10) // Adjust as needed

	response, err := call.Do()
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Error making API call: %v", err)
	}

	fmt.Printf("Search results for '%s':\n", query)
	for _, item := range response.Items {
		switch item.Id.Kind {
		case "youtube#video":
			fmt.Printf("  Video: %s (%s)\n", item.Snippet.Title, item.Id.VideoId)
		case "youtube#channel":
			fmt.Printf("  Channel: %s (%s)\n", item.Snippet.Title, item.Id.ChannelId)
		case "youtube#playlist":
			fmt.Printf("  Playlist: %s (%s)\n", item.Snippet.Title, item.Id.PlaylistId)
		}
	}
}

func main() {
	// Assume getClient() from the authorization example is available and returns an authenticated *http.Client
	// ctx := context.Background()
	// client, err := getClient(ctx)
	// if err != nil {
	// 	log.Fatalf("Unable to get authenticated client: %v", err)
	// }
	// search(client)
	fmt.Println("This is a placeholder. Call search with an authenticated client and -query flag.")
}

```

### I18nLanguages: list

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/docs/i18nLanguages/list

Returns a list of application languages that the YouTube website supports. This method has a quota cost of 1 unit.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/i18nLanguages

### Description
Returns a list of application languages that the YouTube website supports.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/i18nLanguages

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - Specifies the `i18nLanguage` resource properties that the API response will include. Set the parameter value to `snippet`.
- **hl** (string) - Optional - Specifies the language that should be used for text values in the API response. The default value is `en_US`.

### Request Body
Do not provide a request body when calling this method.

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **kind** (string) - Identifies the API resource's type. The value will be `youtube#i18nLanguageListResponse`.
- **etag** (etag) - The Etag of this resource.
- **items[]** (list) - A list of supported i18n languages. In this map, the i18n language ID is the map key, and its value is the corresponding `i18nLanguage` resource.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "kind": "youtube#i18nLanguageListResponse",
  "etag": "etag",
  "items": [
    {
      "kind": "youtube#i18nLanguage",
      "etag": "etag",
      "id": "en",
      "snippet": {
        "value": "English",
        "rtl": false
      }
    }
  ]
}
```
```

### YouTube Data API v3: Methods Supporting 'onBehalfOfContentOwner'

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=vi

Several methods now support the 'onBehalfOfContentOwner' parameter. This parameter allows the authenticated user to act on behalf of the specified content owner when performing actions like inserting channel banners, updating channels, or managing video ratings.

```json
{
  "methods": [
    "channelBanners.insert",
    "channels.update",
    "videos.getRating",
    "videos.rate"
  ],
  "parameter": {
    "name": "onBehalfOfContentOwner",
    "type": "string",
    "description": "The ID of the content owner on whose behalf the request is being made.",
    "required": false,
    "location": "query"
  }
}
```

### Manage Captions with onBehalfOfContentOwner (YouTube Data API v3)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=vi

The captions.delete, captions.download, captions.insert, captions.list, and captions.update methods now support the 'onBehalfOfContentOwner' parameter. Requests using this parameter require authorization with the 'https://www.googleapis.com/auth/youtubepartner' scope.

```http
POST /youtube/v3/captions?onBehalfOfContentOwner=YOUR_CONTENT_OWNER_ID HTTP/1.1
Host: www.googleapis.com
Authorization: Bearer YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN
Content-Type: application/json

{
  "snippet": {
    "videoId": "VIDEO_ID",
    "language": "en"
  }
}
```

### GET /youtube/v3/search - Order Parameter Update

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-cn

The 'order' parameter for the search.list method has been updated to clarify behavior when sorting live broadcasts by 'viewCount'. Results are sorted by concurrent viewers during ongoing broadcasts.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/search

### Description
Updates to the `search.list` method's `order` parameter note that if live broadcasts are sorted by `viewCount`, the API results are sorted by the broadcasts' number of concurrent viewers while they are ongoing.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/search

### Query Parameters
- **order** (string) - Optional - Specifies the order of search results. If set to `viewCount` for live broadcasts, results are sorted by concurrent viewers.
```

### Retrieve My Uploads

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/code_samples/dotnet

Retrieves a list of videos uploaded to the authenticated user's channel using the `playlistItems.list` and `channels.list` methods.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/playlistItems

### Description
Retrieves a list of videos uploaded to the authenticated user's channel.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/playlistItems

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - The part parameter specifies the playlist item properties that the API response should include. Set to "snippet" to include these.
- **channelId** (string) - Required - The ID of the channel whose uploads you want to retrieve. Use 'UCxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx' for the authenticated user's channel.
- **maxResults** (integer) - Optional - The maximum number of results to return.
- **pageToken** (string) - Optional - The page token, if any, of the next page of results.

### Request Example
```
GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/playlistItems?part=snippet&channelId=UCxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx&maxResults=25
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **items** (array) - A list of playlist items.
  - **snippet.title** (string) - The title of the video.
  - **snippet.resourceId.videoId** (string) - The ID of the video.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "kind": "youtube#playlistItemListResponse",
  "etag": "_abcdefg1234567890",
  "items": [
    {
      "kind": "youtube#playlistItem",
      "etag": "_abcdefg1234567890",
      "id": "abcdefg1234567890",
      "snippet": {
        "publishedAt": "2023-01-01T12:00:00Z",
        "channelId": "UCxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx",
        "title": "My First Upload",
        "description": "This is my first video.",
        "thumbnails": {
          "default": {
            "url": "https://i.ytimg.com/vi/abcdefg123/default.jpg",
            "width": 120,
            "height": 90
          }
        },
        "resourceId": {
          "kind": "youtube#video",
          "videoId": "abcdefg1234567890"
        },
        "videoOwnerChannelTitle": "Example Channel",
        "videoOwnerChannelId": "UCxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx"
      }
    }
  ],
  "pageInfo": {
    "totalResults": 100,
    "resultsPerPage": 25
  }
}
```
```

### List Activities

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/docs/activities/list

Retrieves a list of activities that match the specified criteria. This endpoint supports various query parameters for filtering and pagination.

```APIDOC
## GET /activities

### Description
Retrieves a list of activities that match the specified criteria. This endpoint supports various query parameters for filtering and pagination.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/activities

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - Specifies a comma-separated list of one or more `activity` resource properties to include in the response. Valid values include `contentDetails`, `id`, `snippet`.
- **channelId** (string) - Required (one of `channelId`, `home`, or `mine`) - Specifies a unique YouTube channel ID. Returns a list of that channel's activities.
- **home** (boolean) - Required (one of `channelId`, `home`, or `mine`) - Deprecated. For authorized requests, retrieves items similar to those a logged-out user would see on the YouTube home page.
- **mine** (boolean) - Required (one of `channelId`, `home`, or `mine`) - For authorized requests, retrieves a feed of the authenticated user's activities.
- **maxResults** (unsigned integer) - Optional - Specifies the maximum number of items to return (0-50). Defaults to 5.
- **pageToken** (string) - Optional - Identifies a specific page in the result set to return.
- **publishedAfter** (datetime) - Optional - Specifies the earliest date and time an activity could have occurred to be included. Format: ISO 8601 (`YYYY-MM-DDThh:mm:ss.sZ`).
- **publishedBefore** (datetime) - Optional - Specifies the date and time before which an activity must have occurred to be excluded. Format: ISO 8601 (`YYYY-MM-DDThh:mm:ss.sZ`).
- **regionCode** (string) - Optional - Instructs the API to return results for the specified country using an ISO 3166-1 alpha-2 code.

### Request Body
Do not provide a request body when calling this method.

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **kind** (string) - Identifies the API resource's type (`youtube#activityListResponse`).
- **etag** (etag) - The Etag of this resource.
- **nextPageToken** (string) - The token for the next page of results.
- **prevPageToken** (string) - The token for the previous page of results.
- **pageInfo** (object) - Encapsulates paging information.
  - **pageInfo.totalResults** (integer) - The total number of results.
  - **pageInfo.resultsPerPage** (integer) - The number of results per page.
- **items** (list) - A list of activities matching the request criteria.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "kind": "youtube#activityListResponse",
  "etag": "etag",
  "nextPageToken": "string",
  "prevPageToken": "string",
  "pageInfo": {
    "totalResults": 100,
    "resultsPerPage": 10
  },
  "items": [
    {
      "kind": "youtube#activity",
      "etag": "etag",
      "id": "activityId",
      "snippet": {
        "publishedAt": "2023-01-01T10:00:00Z",
        "channelId": "channelId",
        "title": "Video Uploaded",
        "description": "User uploaded a new video.",
        "thumbnails": {},
        "channelTitle": "Channel Name",
        "type": "upload"
      },
      "contentDetails": {}
    }
  ]
}
```
```

### YouTube Data API v3 - Quota Usage

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/getting-started

This section explains how the quota system works in the YouTube Data API v3, including default limits, operation costs, and how to monitor and request quota extensions.

```APIDOC
## Quota Usage

### Description
The YouTube Data API v3 operates on a quota system to manage resource consumption and prevent abuse. Understanding quota usage is crucial for developing stable and scalable applications.

### Quota System Basics
*   **Default Limits**: Each project is allocated a default daily quota. This limit can be viewed and managed in the Google Developers Console.
*   **Operation Costs**: Different API operations consume varying amounts of quota. Read operations generally cost less than write operations.
*   **Monitoring**: The Google Developers Console provides tools to monitor your API usage and quota consumption in real-time.
*   **Quota Extensions**: If your application requires higher quota limits, you can submit a request for an increase through the Google Developers Console.

### Calculating Quota Usage
*   Each API request consumes a certain number of quota units. The exact cost for each operation is documented in the API reference.
*   For example, a `videos.list` request might cost 1 quota unit, while a `videos.insert` request could cost 1600 quota units.

### Best Practices
*   **Cache Data**: Cache frequently accessed data to reduce the number of API calls.
*   **Use `part` and `fields` parameters**: Retrieve only the data you need to minimize response size and potentially reduce quota usage for complex requests.
*   **Handle Quota Exceeded Errors**: Implement logic to gracefully handle `403 Forbidden` errors that occur when quota limits are reached.
```

### Using the 'part' Parameter

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/getting-started

The 'part' parameter is mandatory for API requests and specifies which top-level resource properties to include in the response. This helps reduce latency and bandwidth by only retrieving necessary metadata.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/videos

### Description
Retrieves a list of videos. The `part` parameter specifies which video resource properties to include in the response.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/youtube/v3/videos`

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - Comma-separated list of video resource properties to include. Possible values include: `snippet`, `contentDetails`, `fileDetails`, `player`, `processingDetails`, `recordingDetails`, `statistics`, `status`, `suggestions`, `topicDetails`.
- **id** (string) - Optional - The ID of the video to retrieve.

### Request Example
```
GET /youtube/v3/videos?part=snippet,statistics&id=dQw4w9WgXcQ
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **items** (array) - An array of video resources.
  - **snippet** (object) - Contains properties like `title`, `description`, `publishedAt`.
  - **statistics** (object) - Contains properties like `viewCount`, `likeCount`.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "items": [
    {
      "snippet": {
        "publishedAt": "2009-03-06T19:44:30.000Z",
        "title": "Rick Astley - Never Gonna Give You Up (Official Music Video)"
      },
      "statistics": {
        "viewCount": "1500000000",
        "likeCount": "10000000"
      }
    }
  ]
}
```
```

### Response

No content is returned upon successful rating.

#### Error Response (500)

  - **message** (string) - A description of the error.

### Response Example

### Get Channel Subscribers (YouTube Data API v3)

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-cn

Previously, `channels.list` with `mySubscribers` was used. This functionality is now deprecated. Use `subscriptions.list` with `mySubscribers` to retrieve a list of subscribers for the authenticated user's channel.

```javascript
gapi.client.subscriptions.list({
  "part": [
    "snippet,subscriberSnippet"
  ],
  "mine": true,
  "mySubscribers": true
}).then(function(response) {
  // Handle the response
  console.log(response.result);
});
```

--------------------------------

### PlaylistItems: insert

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/docs/playlistItems/insert

Adds a resource to a playlist. This operation has a quota cost of 50 units.

```APIDOC
## POST /youtube/v3/playlistItems

### Description
Adds a resource to a playlist. Stay organized with collections by saving and categorizing content based on your preferences.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/playlistItems

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required - Identifies the properties that the write operation will set as well as the properties that the API response will include. Valid values are `contentDetails`, `id`, `snippet`, `status`.
- **onBehalfOfContentOwner** (string) - Optional - Indicates that the request's authorization credentials identify a YouTube CMS user who is acting on behalf of the content owner specified in the parameter value. Intended for YouTube content partners.

#### Request Body
- **snippet.playlistId** (string) - Required - The ID of the playlist to which the item will be added.
- **snippet.resourceId** (object) - Required - The resource ID object, containing the ID of the video or other resource to add.
  - **kind** (string) - Optional - The kind of resource, e.g. 'youtube#video'.
  - **videoId** (string) - Required if kind is 'youtube#video' - The ID of the video to add.
- **snippet.position** (integer) - Optional - The position at which to insert the item in the playlist. If omitted, the item will be added to the end of the playlist.
- **contentDetails.note** (string) - Optional - A note to be associated with the playlist item.
- **contentDetails.startAt** (string) - Optional - The time, measured in seconds from the start of the video, to start playing the video. Any value specified is converted to milliseconds.
- **contentDetails.endAt** (string) - Optional - The time, measured in seconds from the start of the video to stop playing the video. Any value specified is converted to milliseconds.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "snippet": {
    "playlistId": "YOUR_PLAYLIST_ID",
    "resourceId": {
      "kind": "youtube#video",
      "videoId": "YOUR_VIDEO_ID"
    }
  }
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
Returns a playlistItem resource in the response body.
- **kind** (string) - Identifies this as a playlist resource. Value is `youtube#playlistItem`.
- **etag** (string) - The ETag of the playlist item.
- **id** (string) - The ID of the playlist item.
- **snippet** (object) - The snippet object contains basic details about the playlist item.
  - **publishedAt** (string) - The date and time that the item was published to the playlist.
  - **channelId** (string) - The ID of the channel that owns the playlist.
  - **title** (string) - The title of the playlist item.
  - **description** (string) - The description of the playlist item.
  - **thumbnails** (object) - The default, medium, and high quality thumbnails for the playlist item.
  - **channelTitle** (string) - The title of the channel that owns the playlist.
  - **resourceId** (object) - The resource ID object, containing the ID of the video or other resource.
    - **kind** (string) - The kind of resource, e.g. 'youtube#video'.
    - **videoId** (string) - The ID of the video.
  - **videoOwnerChannelId** (string) - The ID of the channel that owns the video.
  - **videoOwnerChannelTitle** (string) - The title of the channel that owns the video.
- **contentDetails** (object) - The contentDetails object contains details about the playlist item's content.
  - **endAt** (string) - The time, measured in seconds from the start of the video, to stop playing the video.
  - **startAt** (string) - The time, measured in seconds from the start of the video, to start playing the video.
  - **note** (string) - A note to be associated with the playlist item.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "kind": "youtube#playlistItem",
  "etag": "YOUR_ETAG",
  "id": "YOUR_PLAYLIST_ITEM_ID",
  "snippet": {
    "publishedAt": "2023-01-01T12:00:00Z",
    "channelId": "YOUR_CHANNEL_ID",
    "title": "Video Title",
    "description": "Video Description",
    "thumbnails": {
      "default": {
        "url": "https://i.ytimg.com/vi/VIDEO_ID/default.jpg",
        "width": 120,
        "height": 90
      },
      "medium": {
        "url": "https://i.ytimg.com/vi/VIDEO_ID/mqdefault.jpg",
        "width": 320,
        "height": 180
      },
      "high": {
        "url": "https://i.ytimg.com/vi/VIDEO_ID/hqdefault.jpg",
        "width": 480,
        "height": 360
      }
    },
    "channelTitle": "Channel Title",
    "resourceId": {
      "kind": "youtube#video",
      "videoId": "YOUR_VIDEO_ID"
    },
    "videoOwnerChannelId": "YOUR_CHANNEL_ID",
    "videoOwnerChannelTitle": "Channel Title"
  },
  "contentDetails": {
    "endAt": "",
    "startAt": "",
    "note": ""
  }
}
```
```

--------------------------------

### playlists.list

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=th

Lists playlists with onBehalfOfContentOwner and onBehalfOfContentOwnerChannel parameters.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/playlists

### Description
Lists playlists with support for onBehalfOfContentOwner and onBehalfOfContentOwnerChannel parameters.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/playlists

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **part** (string) - Required -  Specifies a comma-separated list of one or more playlist resource properties that the API response will include.
- **channelId** (string) - Optional -  The channelId parameter specifies a YouTube channel ID. The API will only return that channel's playlists.
- **onBehalfOfContentOwner** (string) - Optional - Note: This parameter is intended exclusively for YouTube content partners.The onBehalfOfContentOwner parameter specifies the YouTube channel ID of the content owner that the service account is acting on behalf of.
- **onBehalfOfContentOwnerChannel** (string) - Optional -  The onBehalfOfContentOwnerChannel parameter specifies the YouTube channel ID of the content owner that the service account is acting on behalf of.

### Request Example
```
GET /youtube/v3/playlists?part=snippet&channelId=UC_x5XG1OV2P6uZZ5FSM9Ttw&onBehalfOfContentOwner=...&onBehalfOfContentOwnerChannel=...
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- Returns a list of playlists based on the specified parameters.

```

--------------------------------

### playlists.insert - Python

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-tw

A Python code sample for creating YouTube playlists using the playlists.insert method. Requires authentication and the Google API client libraries for Python.

```Python
# Example of using playlists.insert in Python
# This would require the Google API Client Library for Python and user authentication.

# from googleapiclient.discovery import build

# youtube = build('youtube', 'v3', developerKey='YOUR_API_KEY') # Or use authenticated client

# playlist_body = {
#     "snippet": {
#         "title": "My New Playlist",
#         "description": "A description for my playlist."
#     },
#     "status": {
#         "privacyStatus": "public"
#     }
# }

# request = youtube.playlists().insert(
#     part="snippet,status",
#     body=playlist_body
# )
# response = request.execute()

# print(response)

```

--------------------------------

### Download Caption Track HTTP Request

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/docs/captions/download

This is the basic HTTP GET request to download a caption track. It requires the `id` of the caption track. Optional parameters `tfmt` and `tlang` can be appended to specify the desired format and language of the caption track, respectively.

```HTTP
GET https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/captions/id
```

--------------------------------

### GET /youtube/v3/search - Updates to search.list method

Source: https://developers.google.com/youtube/v3/revision_history_hl=zh-tw

The search.list method's 'order' parameter has been updated to clarify sorting behavior for live broadcasts by 'viewCount'. The 'relatedToVideoId' parameter also has updated restrictions on other supported parameters.

```APIDOC
## GET /youtube/v3/search

### Description
This endpoint allows searching for resources on YouTube. Updates have been made to the `order` and `relatedToVideoId` parameters.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/youtube/v3/search

### Query Parameters
- **order** (string) - Specifies the order of search results. If sorting live broadcasts by `viewCount`, results are sorted by concurrent viewers while ongoing.
- **relatedToVideoId** (string) - Returns results related to the specified video. If set, only `part`, `maxResults`, `pageToken`, `regionCode`, `relevanceLanguage`, `safeSearch`, `type` (must be `video`), and `fields` are supported.
- **part** (string) - Specifies the parts of the search resource that should be included in the response.
- **maxResults** (integer) - The maximum number of results to return.
- **pageToken** (string) - The page token to retrieve the next page of results.
- **regionCode** (string) - Returns search results for a specific region.
- **relevanceLanguage** (string) - Returns search results that are in a particular language.
- **safeSearch** (string) - Indicates whether to use Safe Search filtering.
- **type** (string) - Specifies the resource type to return. Must be `video` when `relatedToVideoId` is set.
- **fields** (string) - Selector specifying which fields to include in a partial response.
```
